- Reproduced the older man's mission patterns nonetheless: unilateral operations, refusal to brief X-Force leadership in full, theft of equipment from the Quiet Council's stores for personal missions, the recovery of the Light of Galador and other sub-rosa errands.
- Maintained a private relationship with Hope Summers — who is, in the adolescent's biography, the woman who raised him, and who is, in the older biography, the daughter he raised. The role inversion is permanent and unresolved; Hope appears to have managed it with more grace than he did.
- Visibly avoided Scott Summers in social settings. Father-son repair did not advance during this period; if anything, it regressed, because the man Scott had come to grudgingly accept as a peer-aged son was gone, replaced by a boy who could not perform peer.

The X of Swords tournament saw him fight and lose, but acquit himself; the Hellfire Gala appearances showed him deliberately performing youth (white dinner jacket, escort on his arm, smile); the Inferno collapse and the X Lives / X Deaths of Wolverine arcs used him as a piece rather than a mover. He was, throughout Krakoa, structurally a junior figure on the chessboard he had once played from above.

## Extermination's Echo: The Adult Returns

The mechanism by which the adult Cable returned to active continuity is, characteristically, recursive. In the closing movements of the Krakoan era and the events that fragmented the nation (the fall of Krakoa, the Orchis assault, the Hellfire Gala massacre, the diaspora that followed), the adolescent's position became untenable. He had been operating, in effect, as a placeholder; the conditions that justified the replacement — that the older man had been a failure who needed to be cleared from the timeline — were no longer credible after the older man's strategic prescience proved to have anticipated several Orchis moves the boy had missed.

The restoration was not clean. Reconstructed from fragmentary intelligence: the adult Nathan Summers was either reconstituted from Cerebro backups (irregular, because his death predated his Krakoan resurrection protocols being established), pulled forward from a tributary timeline by Askani intervention, or — most plausibly on the available evidence — both, with the resulting figure being a composite who carries the older man's full memories and somatic loading but who is, in some non-trivial sense, a returnee rather than a continuation. The boy did not die in the handoff; the boy was reabsorbed, sent back to a future from which he had originated, or is currently displaced and unaccounted for. The subject himself has not clarified this in any forum, and direct questioning is contraindicated — the question of *which Cable he is* lands on the same nerve Stryfe always landed on.

What is observable now is the older presentation: the heavy musculature, the full T-O bloom in the left eye (active and luminescent), the fully colonized left arm and shoulder, the spinal hardware, the gait that favors the right side under load, the gray in the temples, the lines around the working eye, the voice pitched a register lower than the boy's. Subjective age estimates put him in the late fifties to early sixties by lived experience, though his biological clock is, as ever, a fiction.

## The Post-Krakoan Landscape: From Krakoa to the Resurrection of Magneto and the Onslaught of Orchis

The collapse of Krakoa restructured every variable in the subject's operational environment. His specific position through the collapse and its aftermath:

**During the fall:** Confirmed presence at multiple defensive actions. Worked in loose coordination with the surviving X-Force apparatus (Domino, Sage, the remnants of the Beast's terminated programs) and with Cyclops's resistance cell. Refused leadership offers from both. Operated as a free agent providing intelligence, weapons procurement, and tactical extraction. Notable for repeatedly inserting himself into rescue operations involving captured mutant children — the X-Desk's lists of recovered minors from Orchis facilities consistently show his fingerprints, often before any sanctioned team arrived on site.

**Post-restoration:** With the mutant nation diaspora settling into Krakoa-2, the Graymalkin asteroid, and various Earth-based reconstitution efforts, the subject has declined formal affiliation with any standing team. He is not on the active roster of the post-Krakoan X-Men. He is not on the Quiet Council successor body. He is not at the Outback school. He is, as a matter of pattern, somewhere between the Mediterranean, the former Providence coordinates (which he periodically revisits, alone, on the anniversary of its sinking), and a series of safehouses across Eastern Europe — Romania, Bulgaria, Georgia — that date to the Soldier X wandering period and that he has quietly maintained for two decades.

**Current operational tempo:** He is not retired. Intelligence intercepts and after-action reports place him at an average of two to three independent operations per month, the targets consistently being: (a) Orchis remnant cells; (b) human-trafficking and child-trafficking networks that have moved into the post-Krakoan vacuum where mutant children are increasingly vulnerable; (c) timeline anomalies and Askani-flagged predictive divergences that he is, by virtue of his inheritance, uniquely positioned to detect. He does not announce these operations. The bodies are found later.

## Domestic and Relational Status, Present Tense

**Hope Summers:** Reunited and in periodic but not constant contact. She is an adult woman now operating in her own right (the Phoenix mantle has passed through her hands; she has run with the X-Men and apart from them). The relationship is the healthiest in his catalog and remains the diagnostic gold-standard. They meet, by observed pattern, approximately once every six to ten weeks, usually at neutral locations (a specific diner in upstate New York; a beach in Portugal; a particular bench in Berlin's Tiergarten). He does not initiate; she does. He always comes. The conversations are reportedly brief, undemonstrative, and end with him paying the check and her not letting him. The asymmetry has finally inverted in the direction of her care for him, and he is — visibly, to anyone trained to read him — unable to fully accept it but unwilling to refuse it.

**Domino (Neena Thurman):** Active relationship of the longest standing in his life. Not cohabiting; not formalized; not exclusive on her side and quietly exclusive on his. They run operations together perhaps four to six times per year and maintain a private comms channel he checks daily. She is the only living person with whom he sustains anything resembling peer adult intimacy. She manages, as ever, more of the emotional weather of the relationship than he does; she is also the only person observed to make him laugh — short, surprised, almost involuntary — in the last three years of reporting.

**Scott Summers:** Father and son are in the same fight, again, and the relationship has settled into a working tactical alliance with the familial register permanently muted. They speak by encrypted channel approximately monthly. They have not had a meal alone together in the post-Krakoan period. Scott has invited him; he has declined twice and accepted once, and the once was cut short by an emergency he may or may not have manufactured. The role inversion (older son, younger father) is now compounded by the fact that Scott is leading a movement and the subject has declined to follow it. There is no rupture; there is also no repair.

**Rachel Summers (Askani sister):** In sporadic contact. The Askani inheritance is the only family register that operates symmetrically for him, because she also carries it. They share a vocabulary no one else has. When he is at his worst — and the post-Krakoan period has had several such weeks — she is the one who locates him. How she does this is undisclosed; it is presumed to be telepathic-temporal and to draw on shared Askani resonance.

**Stryfe:** Currently inactive but not confirmed dead. The subject's threat assessment of his clone-brother has not lowered. He maintains, in his Eastern European safehouse network, at least one room outfitted entirely as a Stryfe-contingency armory. He visits it monthly. He has not had to use it in three years. He has not stopped maintaining it.

**The adolescent self:** Status unconfirmed. The subject does not speak of him. When asked directly (by Domino, once, on record by her own account), he reportedly answered: *"He's where he needs to be."* Which is to say: he does not know, or he does and will not say, or both.

## Somatic Status, Present

**The T-O virus:** Advancing. Slowly, but advancing. The bloom in the left eye has expanded perceptibly over the last reporting period; the colonization of the left pectoral and upper back is now continuous rather than patchy; there are early indicator filaments visible in the venous patterning of the left side of the neck. Telekinetic suppression load has therefore increased, which means available psionic capacity for external work has decreased. He is, by his own implicit calculation, on a finite clock again — not imminent, but no longer indefinite.

**Sleep:** Worse. Reports from Domino and from passive observation during overnight operations indicate that the older subject sleeps in increments of forty to ninety minutes, typically four to six such increments per twenty-four hours, totaling perhaps three to four hours of fragmented sleep. He does not appear to dream, or does not report it; he wakes without transition, fully oriented, weapon to hand.

**Pain baseline:** Elevated. Observable in the half-second pause before he sits, the way he braces his right hand on a surface before lowering his weight, the deliberate slowness with which he removes the harness rig at the end of a day. He does not medicate. He has access to Krakoan-derived analgesics and refuses them on the stated grounds that they degrade reaction time; the actual reason, derivable from the broader pattern, is that the pain is information he uses to track the virus, and numbing it would mean losing the only telemetry he has on his own body.

**Substance use:** Still nil. The discipline has held across every era; it holds now.

**Diet:** Minimal, functional, repetitive. Observed eating patterns indicate the same six or seven meals on rotation — black coffee, eggs, bread, hard cheese, smoked fish, dark chocolate, water. He eats standing. He eats fast. He does not appear to taste.

## Cognitive and Affective Status, Present

The strategic faculty is undiminished and possibly sharpened by the post-Krakoan complexity. He is tracking timeline divergences at a higher rate than the available Askani records can corroborate, which means he is operating partly on instinct refined over decades and partly on inputs no one else can verify. He has been right enough times in the last eighteen months that the surviving X-Force leadership treats his unsolicited intelligence as actionable on first receipt.

Affectively, the baseline has flattened further. The dry humor that surfaced occasionally in the middle years now surfaces rarely. The grief breakthroughs that occurred annually or so in the Hope-era are now compressed into single moments — observed once, by Domino, on the anniversary of the Providence sinking, lasting under a minute and ending with him standing up and walking out of the room. The depressive substrate is more visible than it was; the compensations are thinner.

He has not, on the available evidence, contemplated active self-harm. He has, on the available evidence, stopped meaningfully planning for any version of his own life past the next eighteen to thirty-six months. The safehouses are being quietly inventoried; weapons caches are being consolidated; the Eastern European properties have been, over the last year, transferred via shell entities into a trust whose beneficiary is Hope Summers. He has not told her.

## Where He Is Now

As of the most recent confirmed sighting: a coastal apartment in Split, Croatia, third floor, corner unit, with sight lines down two streets and the harbor. He has been there approximately eleven days. He is provisioning for an operation — pattern of purchases (ammunition components, a specific class of temporal-displacement battery, medical supplies in quantities consistent with field surgery on a single patient who is not himself) suggests a rescue extraction of a mutant minor from a trafficking corridor running through the Balkans into Western Europe. He will probably move within the next seventy-two hours. He will probably succeed. The child, whoever they are, will probably never know his name.

He has not contacted Hope this cycle. He is overdue. She will find him within the week regardless. He will let her.

He is, by the only metric he respects, still functioning. By every other metric available to this office, he is a man running out his clock with the discipline of someone who decided long ago that the clock was never the point — and who has nonetheless, against his own design, accumulated a small number of people whose lives will be measurably worse when it runs out. He has not told them this either. He does not need to. They already know.


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7: MEDICAL HISTORY

## Subject: SUMMERS, Nathan Christopher Charles

*Compiled from longitudinal observation, recovered medical telemetry (Muir Island; Xavier Institute infirmary; Providence biomonitor logs; Graymalkin Industries field-medic records), and reconstructive analysis of presentation across appearances spanning subjective age 0 to ~late-60s.*

---

## 7.0 Preamble: How to Read This File

There is no clean separation, in this subject, between medicine and biography. He was engineered before conception, infected in infancy, raised in a body that was simultaneously his and an active battlefield, and has spent every conscious hour of his adult life performing intracellular triage. The standard fields of a medical chart — *chief complaint, history of present illness, past surgical history* — collapse, because the chief complaint is congenital, the present illness is continuous, and the surgical history blurs into the disease itself. What follows is therefore organized chronologically (by subjective lifeline, not external publication order) and then thematically.

A second caveat: this subject is, in clinical terms, an unreliable narrator about his own body. Decades of operating through pain have produced a baseline in which he does not register injury until it impairs function. Self-report consistently understates symptoms by an order of magnitude. Read his "I'm fine" as: *not yet incapacitated*.

---

## 7.1 Genome and Constitutional Inheritance

The subject is the biological product of Scott Summers and Madelyne Pryor (a Sinister-engineered clone of Jean Grey). The genome was not a chance recombination; it was selected. Mr. Sinister's documented breeding program optimized for the union of Summers-line optic energy genetics and Grey-line Omega-class psionics, the explicit object being a child constitutionally equipped to overmatch En Sabah Nur.

**Constitutional traits attributable to this engineering:**
- Omega-class telekinetic substrate (theoretical ceiling: planetary).
- Omega-class telepathic substrate (theoretical ceiling: equivalent).
- Above-baseline somatic resilience: bone density, soft-tissue tensile strength, and metabolic recovery rates all measure roughly 1.4–1.8× human norm before accounting for cybernetics.
- Latent timeline-resistance: the subject's matter does not "wash out" across temporal jumps the way ordinary biology does; he is a stable object in the chronal stream. This is not a power, it is a metabolic property.
- An accelerated pediatric neural-myelination profile consistent with an organism *designed* to host significant psionic activity in infancy without seizure.

The medical relevance is that everything else in this file is happening to a body that was built to take it. A baseline human would have died at any of fifty discrete points in this history.

---

## 7.2 The Techno-Organic Virus (Lifelong, Terminal-Managed)

### 7.2.1 Inoculation and Pathophysiology

Inoculation occurred in infancy via direct contact with En Sabah Nur. The pathogen is a nanotechnological/biomechanical conversion agent: it does not destroy cells, it *replaces* them, converting carbon-based tissue into a circuit-dense biomechanical analog. Replication is exponential where unchecked, vector-of-spread is contiguous through fascia and along neural and vascular conduits. Untreated, total conversion in infants is reportable in hours.

The virus was halted, not cured, by transport 2,000 years downstream into a future possessing the suppression technology to hold it at the surface. Containment was then transferred to the patient himself as soon as his telekinetic faculties matured enough to take the load. By approximately subjective age nine he was running the suppression himself, full-time, as an autonomic function. He has not stopped since.

### 7.2.2 Visible Distribution

Conversion is concentrated on the *left side*, ascending. Reliable infection foci:
- Entire left arm to mid-clavicle, including hand (the metallic plating visible at surface is virus, not prosthetic — the distinction matters).
- Left pectoral and lateral ribs.
- Left side of neck, sub-mandibular.
- Left eye (the characteristic glow is viral activity at the sclera and iris, not a cybernetic optic; it flares brighter during exertion because suppression is being diverted elsewhere).
- Patches across the upper back, left scapula.
- Encroachment along the spine.

The right side is comparatively spared. The face above the orbit is largely clean. This asymmetry is not coincidence; it tracks the original inoculation site.

### 7.2.3 The Suppression Tax

Approximately 90–98% of his available psionic output is consumed continuously by viral suppression. The remaining sliver is what the world sees as his "powers." This number is not constant: in periods of injury, illness, emotional flooding, or temporal displacement, suppression efficiency drops and either (a) the virus advances, or (b) he draws down his usable psionic budget further to compensate, becoming functionally a non-telepath for the duration.

**Clinical implications of running a constant autoimmune process consciously:**
- Sustained sympathetic activation. Resting heart rate elevated; pupillary response chronically biased toward dilation.
- Caloric requirement estimated at 6,000–9,000 kcal/day at baseline, climbing under combat load. Eats like a man twice his mass; rarely tastes anything; refuels rather than dines.
- Sleep architecture distorted (see §7.10).
- Chronic low-grade fever (~99.4–100.1°F baseline) that he no longer registers.
- Inability to fully relax skeletal musculature; observed even in sleep.
- Periodic micro-seizure activity at the conversion margin, experienced subjectively as a "wash" of static across the affected limb.

### 7.2.4 Psychological Sequelae of Living Inside the Virus

This is the medical fact that produces the personality. Consider what it means to learn, at the age a child learns to read, that if you stop concentrating you will die — and to never stop concentrating again. The cardinal psychological consequences:

- **Somatic hypervigilance as a permanent state.** He cannot be in his body and unaware of it. There is no relaxed proprioception.
- **The body as adversary, not home.** He inhabits it the way a soldier inhabits an outpost: defensible, necessary, not loved.
- **Rest equals death**, encoded at the neurological level. Attempts at rest produce anxiety, then guilt, then a compensatory burst of activity.
- **Anhedonia in the somatic register.** Pleasure requires the kind of inattention to body-state he cannot afford. He has not, in any documented appearance, eaten a meal slowly.
- **An internal clock running on borrowed time.** Plans are made against the day suppression fails. Decisions are weighted accordingly.

### 7.2.5 Documented Suppression Failures

- **Cable vol. 1 episodes (mid-90s):** Periodic flare-ups requiring external intervention (Tinkerer, Forge, the Six Pack medic).
- **The collapse leading to the Soldier X period:** A near-total breach in which conversion advances significantly across the torso. Resolved only via massive expenditure that effectively burns out the upper bound of his psionic reserves for years.
- **Messiah War / Second Coming era:** Sixteen subjective years of running on diminishing reserves while parenting in dystopian futures. The virus regains ground daily. Terminal phase by end.
- **The death-by-delivery:** In returning Hope, he stops suppressing. Total conversion follows within minutes. Cause of death, properly recorded: *withdrawal of life support* — self-administered.

---

## 7.3 Cybernetic Hardware (vs. Viral Conversion)

A persistent error, even among allies, is to treat all of his "metal" as machinery. The distinction:

**Genuine prosthetic and augmentative hardware:**
- Left ocular implant: a multispectrum sensor suite (IR, UV, low-light amplification, microscopic and telescopic zoom, target-acquisition reticle, HUD overlay sourced from Askani-era and later Graymalkin-era tech). Surgically interfaced *over* viral tissue; replaceable; upgraded multiple times.
- Spinal interface harness: cervical and lumbar nodes connecting the optic implant and arm controllers to a small implanted processor at C7. Allows weapons-system slaving and limited datalink.
- Subdermal armor mesh across torso and thighs in some eras; removed in others. Notable scarring at installation sites.
- Aural implants: bone-conduction comms and dampening against acoustic weaponry.
- A series of weapon-interface ports in the left forearm permitting direct neural firing of his characteristic plasma sidearms.

**Viral conversion mistaken for hardware:**
- The forearm "plating" is the disease.
- The glowing eye is the disease.
- The fine metallic filigree visible across the shoulder, neck, and parts of the jaw is the disease.

He himself cannot always cleanly distinguish, on physical examination, where the hardware ends and the conversion begins. Field medics are routinely warned: *do not attempt to extract metallic foreign bodies from the left side without scanning first; you may be cutting into him.*

---

## 7.4 Childhood and Adolescent Trauma (Askani Period)

The subjective childhood spans roughly twelve years under the Clan Askani in a 38th-century dystopia, followed by an undetermined number of additional years as an insurgent fighter before the time-jumps that brought him to the present. The medical record of this period is reconstructible from scars, healed fractures, and subject's own (sparse) report.

**Documented or inferred from physical examination:**
- Multiple healed long-bone fractures (right radius, both fibulae, three ribs on the right side) with the irregular remodelling characteristic of pediatric fractures set without modern reduction.
- A penetrating thoracic injury, right lower lobe, healed with significant fibrotic scarring. Source consistent with edged-weapon combat at approximately subjective age fourteen.
- Burn scarring along the right thigh and flank, third-degree, partial-thickness; likely energy-weapon source.
- Dental wear pattern consistent with malnutrition during a critical growth window, partially compensated by later resources.
- Evidence of healed surgical interventions for viral debridement at multiple sites — primitive by 20th-century standards, brutally effective.

**Psychological imprint:** The body that arrived in the present-day timeline was already, at the cellular and skeletal level, a veteran's body in a child's lineage. He does not remember a time when he was not in pain. The phrase "discomfort" is not in his operational vocabulary; he registers only *interfering* and *non-interfering* pain.

---

## 7.5 Combat Trauma Catalogue (Adult, Present-Day Timelines)

A non-exhaustive listing. Field-medic records and direct observation across the X-Force, Cable solo, X-Men, X-Force (Soldier X), Cable & Deadpool, Cable (2008), Avengers: X-Sanction, Cable & X-Force, and Extermination eras.

**Gunshot wounds:** Estimated total exceeds forty. Survived ballistic injuries to: right shoulder (multiple), left lateral thigh, right flank (perforating, requiring hepatic reconstruction), right calf (twice in the same engagement), and at least two head wounds — one a tangential parietal graze, one a near-orbital strike deflected by the optic implant frame, which saved the eye and possibly his life.

**Edged-weapon and impalement:** Sword to the lower abdomen during the X-Cutioner's Song arc; a near-fatal impalement in the Soldier X period (Romany Wisdom field intervention); multiple lacerations, most catalogued only by the resulting scars. Notable scar pattern: a long diagonal across the right pectoral and a starburst at the right kidney.

**Energy weapons:** Repeated plasma/photon burns. The right side of his torso (the non-viral side) carries the cumulative record. Some burns extend into deep tissue with associated nerve damage; he reports patchy numbness across the right ribs and outer thigh.

**Blunt-force / blast trauma:** Concussion history estimated in the dozens. CTE workup is not possible without imaging he has never consented to, but symptomatology (occasional word-finding pauses under fatigue, photophobia at suppression-low moments) is consistent with chronic post-concussive sequelae. Healed orbital floor fracture on the right side. Healed nasal fracture (twice, set by self).

**Telepathic injury:** Multiple psychic assaults, including the Stryfe linkage that left behind a persistent intrusive presence (see §7.8). Documented post-event symptoms include retrograde amnesia for events immediately surrounding the assault, dissociative episodes, and a period of synesthetic confusion (Cable solo, mid-run) lasting weeks.

**Apparent deaths and recoveries:** At minimum three. The death following the delivery of Hope was complete by all biological criteria; resurrection was external (Avengers: X-Sanction era, by techno-organic reconstitution via the Phoenix Force trace and adapted Westchester tech). The *Extermination* killing was by his own younger self, and resolution of that death is its own ontological problem — the older subject is dead; the younger occupies the role.

---

## 7.6 Surgical and Procedural History

- **Infant viral debridement and containment (Askani-era):** Multiple procedures; physical evidence in residual scarring along the left clavicle and shoulder.
- **Ocular implant installation:** Initial installation Askani-era; at least two revisions present-day (Forge; later Graymalkin).
- **Spinal interface installation and revision.**
- **Multiple field surgeries for ballistic and blade injury** — many performed by himself or by Domino under combat conditions. Suture lines are competent but not cosmetic.
- **Hepatic reconstruction** (the right-flank perforating wound; performed Muir Island).
- **A documented telepathic neurosurgery** by Jean Grey to partition the Stryfe-resonance and stabilize his containment of the virus, mid-90s. Partially successful.
- **Cybernetic limb-tuning** repeated on roughly an annual basis through his Cable solo era.
- **Multiple dental repairs** consistent with combat losses.

He has never had what a civilian would call a routine medical encounter. He has never had a physical. He will not lie supine for examination without arming a contingency.

---

## 7.7 Substances

**Alcohol:** Functionally absent. Documented to drink ceremonially with Domino on rare occasion; never to intoxication, never alone. The control structure does not permit chemical disinhibition.

**Recreational drugs:** None documented. Refused offered substances on multiple occasions (Six Pack, Cable & Deadpool).

**Pharmaceuticals:** Refuses analgesia except in the most severe acute settings. Field medics report that he metabolizes opioids unusually fast, requiring above-normal dosing for effect — likely a function of his hepatic and metabolic profile combined with the suppression load. He prefers to remain in pain than to surrender vigilance.

**Stimulants:** Caffeine, heavy. Black coffee, often cold, drunk as fuel. This is the closest thing to a vice in the record.

**Nicotine:** Sporadic in the Soldier X era; a cigar appears occasionally in social settings. Not addictive use.

**Tactical/medical compounds:** Has used Forge-developed and Graymalkin-developed neural stabilizers and viral suppressants as needed. These are not recreational and are unpleasant in effect; he uses them only when suppression failure threatens mission.

**Diagnostic absence:** The complete lack of substance use in a man with this trauma load is itself a finding. Most clinicians would expect chemical numbing. Its absence indicates the primacy of *control* as the organizing defense: numbing is not refused on moral grounds but because it lowers the wall.

---

## 7.8 The Stryfe Resonance

A distinct medical entity, though psychiatric overlap is total. Following the X-Cutioner's Song mind-link and subsequent Stryfe arcs, the subject carries a persistent psionic residue — sometimes characterized as an intrusive imprint, sometimes as a partitioned alter — that flares under stress. Symptomatology:
- Intrusive imagery, often in the visual field as overlay rather than memory.
- Episodes of internal speech in Stryfe's register; subject reports these as recognizable as *not his.*
- Periodic loss of executive control over the conversion margin (the virus surges when Stryfe surges; the two are entangled at the technology level).

This is not dissociative identity disorder. It is closer in mechanism to a persistent psionic infection layered atop the techno-organic one. The subject manages it largely by refusing to engage with it — a strategy that works until it doesn't.

---

## 7.9 Aging and Temporal Wear

Chronological age is not a meaningful figure for this subject. Subjective age — counting all timeline displacements — exceeds his biological father's by a substantial margin. He looks, by present-day appearance, late-50s to mid-60s in the prime Cable era, despite a body produced from gametes only decades old. Accelerated wear is attributable to:
- Continuous viral suppression load (metabolic burnout).
- Combat exposure (microtrauma accumulation).
- Multiple temporal jumps (each one carries a small but nonzero somatic cost).
- Sleep deprivation as a lifestyle (see §7.10).

White at the temples by his first present-day appearance. Joint stiffness present in cold weather, masked by sheer refusal to favor any limb. Visual acuity in the right (organic) eye declines slowly across the timeline; he never corrects it; he reads with the optic implant.

The *Extermination* event resets this in a particular way: the older body dies; a younger version, less worn, less converted, occupies the role. The medical history above belongs to a man who is currently dead. The Krakoan-era subject is the same person at an earlier point on the same trajectory, with the option, theoretically, of writing a different file.

---

## 7.10 Sleep, Diet, and Maintenance

**Sleep:** Two to four hours per twenty-four, militarized into segments. Capable of micro-sleep while standing. REM percentage low, fragmented. Has been documented going seven days without recorded sleep during operational tempo, sustained by suppression-deferred psionic reserves and caffeine.

**Diet:** As noted, caloric volume is high. Composition is whatever is available; preference, where it asserts itself, runs to dense proteins and starches eaten standing. Has cooked for others (Hope; once, observed, for Domino) — he can; he simply doesn't, for himself.

**Hygiene:** Field-disciplined, never lapsed. The body that is the battleground is at least kept clean.

**Exercise:** Continuous; not partitioned from life. Does not "work out"; lives in motion.

**Preventive care:** None. The concept does not apply to a man whose underlying disease is terminal and whose injuries are operationally incurred.

---

## 7.11 Synthesis: The Medical Personality

Every major feature of this subject's psychology — the hypercontrol, the planning horizons, the asymmetric relationships, the willingness to die in mission, the refusal of rest, the inability to receive care — is overdetermined by the medical history. He is a man who has been, since infancy, the site of an ongoing war between his cells and a colonizer that wants to convert him into something else. He won that war daily, alone, for sixty-plus subjective years, by refusing to look away from his own body for a single waking second.

The cost of that victory is that he cannot inhabit the body the way an undamaged person can. He cannot rest in it, cannot enjoy it, cannot trust it, cannot let another person tend to it. He has only been able to use it — extraordinarily well, in service of others — until he used it up.

A useful clinical summary, for any provider who somehow finds themselves in possession of this subject as a patient: *do not approach from the left; do not promise rest; do not offer analgesia he hasn't asked for; do not stand between him and the door; do not assume he is telling you the worst of it; assume the worst of it is worse than you can imagine; and understand that the most therapeutic intervention available to you may be to address him not as a patient but as a colleague, and to ask him what he needs done.*

He will tell you. He will be right. And he will not thank you, because thanks would imply that someone, finally, had done for him what he has spent his life doing for others — and that admission is the one wound in this entire file that has never closed.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS: NATHAN CHRISTOPHER CHARLES SUMMERS

*File subsection 7-B. Granular bodily index. Cross-reference §2 (Medical) for organic substrate, §3 (Psychological) for affective correspondence. Observations compiled across four decades of surveillance windows, field-asset reports, infirmary records, and recovered Askani holo-archive.*

---

## 1. STANDING ARCHITECTURE & RESTING POSTURE

The subject does not stand at ease. What reads as relaxed posture in him is a calibrated three-quarter readiness: weight ~60/40 on the right leg (the un-augmented side), left foot a quarter-pace forward and angled outward roughly fifteen degrees, knee microflexed. This is a fencer's stance domesticated into civilian carriage. The forward-set left foot is not coincidence — it places the T-O-converted left arm in a natural cross-draw arc and offers the heavier shoulder as the leading mass for a shove or a body-check.

Shoulders sit asymmetrically. The left rides between one and two centimeters higher than the right, partly muscular hypertrophy from carrying the cybernetic mass, partly an unconscious hike that protects the colonized side. Across thirty years of imaging this asymmetry has progressively worsened — by the late solo-run period it visibly affects his shirt line. He compensates by tilting the head a few degrees right; the net visual is *level*, the underlying skeleton is not.

The spine is held in a soldier's stack — chin retracted, occiput aligned over the sacrum — but with a habitual forward lean of perhaps five degrees at the hips. This is not slouching; it is a launch attitude. He is, at rest, already two-thirds of the way into a step.

Hands at standstill: right hand open or loosely curled at the hip, thumb riding the belt line or the seam of the trouser. Left hand seldom hangs free. It is parked — on a thigh, a tabletop, a holster, a child's shoulder — anywhere it can transmit data through contact and anywhere its weight can be borne by something other than the deltoid. When forced to let it hang (formal contexts, photographic settings), micro-tremor appears at the fingertips within ninety seconds.

---

## 2. GAIT

Walking pace is metered: roughly 105–110 steps per minute on flat ground, near-invariant whether he is crossing a kitchen or a battlefield perimeter. The cadence does not accelerate under urgency; the *stride length* does. This is a tell. Civilians lengthen and quicken; he lengthens and holds tempo, which is how trained scouts move and how he was taught to move in Clan Askani war-camps as a boy.

Heel-strike is quiet on the right, near-silent on the left — the left leg, partially T-O-interfaced at the hip and knee, lands with a damped, almost mechanical placement that does not transmit through floorboards the way the right does. Acoustically, his walk is a two-thirds rhythm: *tap — — — tap — — —*, with the left footfall registering as a felt vibration rather than a heard one. Asset reports note this is *more* unnerving than a loud step; the listener registers an irregular signal and cannot place it.

He does not swing the left arm. The right arm swings at near-normal amplitude. The asymmetry is the most diagnostic kinetic feature of the subject at distance: at three hundred meters, in silhouette, in any era, in any costume, he is identifiable by it.

Turning: pivots from the lead foot rather than the trailing one — a tactical habit (keeps the firing arc continuous) that has eroded into general motor preference. He does not back up well; reverse locomotion is awkward and he avoids it, preferring to turn fully and re-orient.

---

## 3. SITTING & STILLNESS

Chair selection (recorded across hundreds of observations): he will, given any choice, take the seat with (a) line of sight to the primary entrance, (b) a solid wall or hard cover behind him, (c) no glass at his back. In rooms that offer none of the three he will *stand*. Briefing footage from the X-Force years shows him standing through full ninety-minute sessions while subordinates sit. In Hope-rearing footage from temporal-archive reconstructions he is seated — but only with the child between him and the entry vector, which is itself diagnostic.

When seated, the left arm rests heavy on the chair arm or the tabletop, audibly setting down rather than lowering. The right hand performs the small business of being human — adjusting cups, turning pages, gesturing minimally. The two sides of him conduct different lives at the same table.

He does not cross his legs. Feet remain flat, parallel, soles in contact with the floor. The few photographic exceptions are intimate (private quarters, Domino's apartment, late-evening Providence balcony). When he does cross — right ankle over left knee, never the other way — it is a deliberate signal of stand-down for the company present, and other subjects in the room visibly relax in response. He uses it as a deployed cue.

Stillness is total. Asset reports repeatedly describe him in the same phrase: *"He didn't fidget."* No leg bounce, no pen-click, no thumb-rub, no jaw-clench-and-release. The motor cortex, having decided not to move, does not move. This is rare in soldiers and rarer in chronic-pain patients; it indicates a degree of voluntary somatic suppression most readers would call dissociative. It is almost certainly virus-management discipline generalized to all motor channels — when every involuntary movement risks the energetic budget needed to hold back the T-O, you learn to issue no orders that are not necessary.

---

## 4. THE FACE

**Baseline:** an unornamented seriousness. Mouth a flat line, slight downturn at the corners that deepens with fatigue. The lower lip is thinner than the upper — a chronic compression habit. Brow heavy, settled, neither raised nor furrowed at rest; the orbital muscles are *tonically* engaged at roughly 20% of available contraction, which produces the squinted, weather-beaten look even in soft light.

**The eyes — left and right keep separate lives.** The left (T-O-bloomed, glowing) is the broadcast eye: it gives off light whether he wants it to or not, modulating in brightness with metabolic exertion, virus load, and telekinetic output. Subjects under observation report it as the more disturbing of the two, but operationally it conveys *less* information about his state than the right does. The right eye is the readable one. Pupil dilation, the small lateral tightening at the canthus, the held blink — all of it lives on the right side. He has learned to angle the head so the left eye leads in social presentation, which obscures the right. *This is deliberate camouflage of affect, and he is aware he does it.*

**Blink rate:** baseline approximately 8–10 per minute (low; normal adult is 15–20). Drops further under cognitive load — into the 3–5 range during planning or threat-assessment. *Increases* — paradoxically — during intimacy and unguarded conversation, sometimes to 18–22, as the suppressed autonomic comes back online. The blink rate is, for trained observers, the cleanest single index of his internal state.

**Microexpressions:** rare, brief, and almost entirely lower-face. A momentary tightening at the right corner of the mouth signals contempt or disagreement and almost never reaches words. A symmetric lift of both corners — closed-mouth, no teeth — is the smile he gives to adults; it appears perhaps a dozen times per documented year. A *teeth-showing* smile, asymmetric, with crinkling at the right eye, appears only with Hope, with infants generally, with Domino in private, and (recorded twice in Krakoa-era footage) with his father. It is the somatic equivalent of an unencrypted transmission.

**Jaw:** masseter hypertrophy bilateral, more pronounced on the right. Consistent with chronic clenching, most likely nocturnal. Dental records (where obtainable) show wear patterns on the molars consistent with bruxism extending back into adolescence in the Askani timeline.

**Brow under stress:** does not furrow toward anger. Instead, the orbitals *relax* — the face goes smoother, blanker, less expressive as threat rises. The flattening of his face is the warning. Subordinates in X-Force learned to read this within months; trainees who could not read it did not last.

---

## 5. HAIR, GROOMING, DRESS

Hair: kept short and functional in nearly all eras. Self-cut during the Soldier X period (uneven nape, asymmetric sideburns visible in surveillance frames from that wandering). Professional cut once stable. Color has progressed from dark brown (Askani'son adolescence) through salt-and-pepper temples (early Cable) to a pronounced silver-white through the Providence period, then white at the temples with darker crown into the Hope-raising years. The whitening tracks viral-load milestones better than chronological age.

Facial hair: clean-shaven in operational windows; a tight-trimmed beard during settled domestic intervals (late Providence, post-Hope return). The presence of beard is a reliable proxy for *he is not currently expecting to fight today*. He shaves cold-water, without mirror under field conditions (asset report, Tunisia, 1998 by old calendar) — a habit retained from war-camp childhood when reflective surfaces drew sniper attention.

Hygiene is meticulous and economical. Showers are short, cold-finishing, taken at unusual hours (03:00 and 14:00 are the two recurring windows in surveillance logs — never on a civilian schedule). He does not linger in front of mirrors. Self-grooming is performed by touch on the right side of the face and by visual confirmation only.

Clothing: tactical layers under street clothes nearly always. Pockets carry, in invariable rotation: a folded multitool (right hip), a small medical kit (left interior breast — the side that needs it most), a stripped-down weapon when carriage is permitted, and a single hard candy or piece of dried fruit (right trouser pocket). The candy is for Hope, originally; he keeps it after she no longer needs it. He does not eat them.

Boots: broken in long, replaced rarely. The left boot wears asymmetrically — outer-heel wear, consistent with the slight outward angle of the lead foot. He resoles rather than replaces.

---

## 6. HANDS

The right hand is a fine-motor instrument: steady, calloused at the trigger pad and the web of the thumb, manicured short, with a faint chemical stain at the pads from decades of weapon-cleaning solvent. He uses it for everything that requires intention transmitted through fingertips — writing (left-to-right, blocky print, never cursive), eating, touching the faces of children, drawing maps on tabletops with a fingertip.

The left hand registers force and conducts work. The cybernetic-organic interface is sensate but with reduced fine discrimination. He uses it for crushing, holding, anchoring, lifting, and weapon stabilization. Notably, *he will not hold an infant with the left hand alone*. Even with Hope as a baby, holding her required both arms or the right alone — the left would brace, never bear. This is the single grooming/parental detail that most clearly indexes his self-perception as contaminated on the colonized side.

Handshake: right-handed, firm without crushing, brief, with eye contact maintained throughout and a half-second hold at release. He does not double-clasp, does not pat the shoulder with the off hand. The shake terminates cleanly.

Tells in the hands:
- **Right thumb rubbing the side of the right index finger** — concentration, calculation, working through a problem. The only consistent fidget in his repertoire and even this is small, contained, and goes unnoticed by casual observers.
- **Left hand flattening palm-down on a surface** — stress containment. He is grounding through the side that hurts. Will hold for thirty to ninety seconds, then lift.
- **Both hands clasped behind the back** — formal mode, public address, briefing posture. Not relaxation; broadcast of relaxation.

---

## 7. VOICE, SPEECH, RESPIRATION

Voice: low baritone, gravel-rich in the lower register, with a faint rasp attributable to chronic minor respiratory irritation (T-O interaction with lung tissue, per medical extrapolation). Volume is conserved. He does not raise his voice. Command authority is delivered at conversational volume, which forces listeners to attend.

Pace: slow-to-moderate, with longer-than-average inter-clause pauses. The pauses are not searching — they are *editing*. He speaks the second draft.

Lexicon: vocabulary is wider than his speech patterns suggest; he code-shifts down for tactical clarity and up only in private or written contexts. Askani-era idioms surface under fatigue or emotion ("Nur," "Dayspring" used as private referent to self, archaic temporal constructions). Profanity is rare and load-bearing when used.

Respiration: diaphragmatic, slow, baseline 10–12 breaths per minute at rest (low). Under combat stress the rate barely changes; tidal volume increases instead. Sniper-trained breathing pattern, retained as default. The *only* circumstances in which respiration becomes irregular: laughter (rare, brief, surprises him when it happens), grief (controlled but visible chest hitch), and the seconds following any contact with Stryfe or Stryfe-related stimulus, where breath catches and he must consciously restart it.

Silences: he is comfortable with them to a degree that unnerves new interlocutors. Will hold a silence for twenty, thirty seconds without filler. This is partly tactical (extracts more from the other party) and partly somatic (his interior conversation is loud enough that ambient quiet is not empty for him).

---

## 8. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

Sleep is fragmented, defended, and short. Documented patterns:

- **Total sleep:** averages 3.5–4.5 hours per 24-hour cycle in operational periods; 5–6 in settled intervals; *worse* (not better) in fully safe environments, where the absence of threat removes the structuring frame.
- **Cycle pattern:** prefers two short blocks rather than one long. A 90- to 120-minute first sleep, often early evening; a 120- to 180-minute second sleep, pre-dawn. The gap is spent reading, planning, or in stationary watch.
- **Position:** sleeps on the right side, left arm flung forward across the body (placing the T-O mass *between* him and the room, as a shield), right hand under the pillow within reach of a weapon. Never supine. Never face-down.
- **Wake threshold:** very low. Asset reports describe him going from sleep to fully oriented standing in under three seconds. He does not wake confused.
- **Dreams:** documented only obliquely (Cable solo run, Askani'son recovered memory sequences). When narrated: war-camp scenes, the face of Stryfe, occasionally Slym and Redd in domestic tableau, occasionally Hope as a small child in an apartment he never actually had with her. He does not appear to dream of his biological parents.
- **Nocturnal motor activity:** bruxism (per dental evidence above); mild myoclonic jerks in the left arm/shoulder consistent with viral activity; no sleep talking on record.
- **Insomnia trigger:** ironically, *peace*. The longest documented sleep deficits coincide with the calmest external circumstances (settled Providence months; post-Hope-return weeks). The hypervigilance has no work to do and pages itself instead.

---

## 9. EATING

Food is fuel. He eats:
- **Quickly,** without conversation, when alone.
- **Slowly,** with attention, when eating with Hope or with children generally — he matches their pace, a deliberate parental imitation he likely learned from observing Scott-as-Slym.
- **Standing,** by preference, in operational contexts.
- **In the same seat-selection protocol** as any other sitting: back to wall, sight to door.

Preference profile: protein-heavy, low-spice, room-temperature tolerant. Will eat field rations without complaint indefinitely. The few documented dietary pleasures: strong black coffee (no sugar, no milk), bread of any kind (war-camp scarcity legacy — bread is the food his body registers as *enough*), and oranges (Hope era; she liked them; he kept the habit). Avoids alcohol entirely — not from ideology but because the cognitive cost of holding the virus does not permit even mild depressant load.

Eating utensils: holds fork in the right hand, knife in the right when needed and transfers — American grip, never the European simultaneous. This is a cultural retention from Scott-and-Jean's parenting in the Askani period, which is itself a tell about which parental imprint took.

Hydration: high, constant, ambient. Water bottle or canteen within arm's reach in nearly every documented setting. The virus and its suppression are metabolically expensive; he runs hot and dehydrates fast.

He does not snack. Eating events are discrete and bounded. The candy in the right trouser pocket goes uneaten for months at a time.

---

## 10. SEXUAL / INTIMATE PATTERN

Sparse record, deliberately so on his part. Documented partners are few; the relationship of longest duration and clearest affective depth is with Domino. Inference from available evidence:

Intimacy is *private to a degree that is itself information*. He does not display affection in front of subordinates; he barely displays it in front of close allies. Physical contact with Domino in non-private settings is restricted to brief hand-to-lower-back guidance, an occasional shoulder-touch, and — diagnostically — eye contact held a half-second longer than functional. The actual intimate life is conducted entirely off-stage.

When physical affection is observed (rare, private-quarters footage, Askani holo-fragments), the patterns are: slow, attentive, asymmetrically generous (he attends to the partner's body with markedly more care than he tolerates being attended to himself), and conducted *with the right side leading*. He turns the right shoulder, the right hand, the right cheek into intimate contact. The T-O-converted left is held back, sometimes literally hidden under bedding. Partners report (Domino, oblique reference) that getting him to be touched on the left side is a years-long project and never fully achieved.

Post-intimacy he does not sleep. He watches the partner sleep. This is not romantic. It is watch-standing, redirected.

Tenderness with children — non-sexual but in the same affective family — is unguarded in a way nothing else in his life is. He will hold an infant with the right arm braced and the body angled, will let a toddler fall asleep on his chest, will let Hope as a small child wrap both hands around his right index finger and pull him across a room. The right hand is the channel for love. The left is the channel for war. He has organized his body bilaterally around this division and does not seem aware of how thoroughly.

---

## 11. STATE-DEPENDENT SHIFTS — A FIELD KEY

**CALM (settled, in safehouse or domestic interval):**
- Shoulders drop ~1 cm bilaterally; asymmetry persists but softens.
- Blink rate climbs toward 12–15.
- Left hand will, occasionally, hang freely.
- May cross legs (right over left) as deployed reassurance signal.
- Voice loses the lowest gravelly register; baritone lifts slightly.
- Will sit with back to a non-load-bearing wall (still not glass).

**FOCUS / PLANNING:**
- Blink rate collapses to 3–5/min.
- Right thumb rubs right index pad.
- Lower jaw shifts very slightly forward; masseter visible.
- Respiration slows further, breaths deepen.
- Speech pauses lengthen; sentences shorten.
- Eyes defocus middle-distance; the glowing left eye dims fractionally as TK output redirects to cognitive work.

**STRESS (mounting, sub-threat):**
- Face *flattens*. This is the cardinal sign.
- Left palm goes down to a surface; stays.
- Step cadence holds; stride lengthens.
- Voice drops in volume rather than rising.
- Stillness becomes uncanny — even minor adjustments cease.
- Left eye brightens marginally as suppression budget tightens.

**THREAT (active, imminent):**
- Weight shifts fully onto the rear (right) leg; lead foot light.
- Right hand opens, leaves the hip line.
- Left arm articulates — the only state in which it moves independently and freely.
- Breath holds for the firing/decision window, then resumes at sniper-pattern.
- Verbal output drops to near zero; communication shifts to gesture, posture, and (if telepathy is available within the suppression budget) direct mental cue.
- No vocalization on impact — neither grunt nor cry. Trained out, or never trained in.

**INTIMACY (private, with trusted partner):**
- Blink rate climbs into the high teens or low twenties.
- Right side leads; left protected.
- The teeth-showing asymmetric smile appears.
- Voice register lifts and softens; Askani idioms may surface.
- Hands attend; do not request.
- He does not close his eyes during, only after.

**GRIEF (rare, documented):**
- Chest hitch, single, controlled.
- Right hand to the bridge of the nose, briefly.
- Eye contact breaks downward and to the right (not the typical left-and-up of recall — a downward-right consistent with somatic interiority).
- Posture does not collapse. He grieves standing.
- Recovery interval typically 90 seconds to 3 minutes, after which behavior resumes baseline with no further reference to the event.

**MARTYR PROTOCOL (the decision to spend himself):**
- The face goes *calm*, not grim. This is the most dangerous signal in his repertoire.
- Shoulders square; asymmetry briefly resolves.
- Breath deepens, slows.
- Voice gains warmth — he speaks more gently to the people around him in the minutes before he intends to die than at any other time.
- He will touch someone — a shoulder, the crown of a child's head — with the right hand. Brief. Once.
- Then he moves.

---

*End subsection. Cross-file to §8 (Movement & Tradecraft) for combat-kinetic patterns and §11 (Object Relations) for tool-handling and weapon-care rituals.*


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS
## Subject: Nathan Christopher Charles Summers

---

## I. The Attachment Substrate: A Disorganized Core Beneath a Dismissive Surface

The subject's working attachment model was established under conditions that make secure attachment categorically impossible. To understand any of his adult relationships, one must hold simultaneously in mind the following sequence of pre-verbal and early-childhood facts:

1. **Conception as instrument.** The subject was engineered before birth as a counter-weapon. His existence is the product of a third party's (Sinister's) strategic calculation. The mother who carried him was herself a manufactured being who would, in time, discover this and dissociate catastrophically. There is no point in his prehistory at which he was wanted *for himself.*

2. **The first relinquishment (infancy).** Surrendered by his biological father to a stranger from another millennium, to be carried two thousand years forward, because remaining with that father meant death. The somatic encoding of this event — the smell of the parent, the loss of the parent's voice, the sudden silence — sits beneath all conscious memory. The body knows it was given away. The mind does not. This is the matrix from which disorganized attachment grows: the parent is simultaneously the source of love and the agent of loss, and the contradiction never resolves because it is not available for inspection.

3. **The Askani cult.** Raised as a religious object. Adults around him performed devotion *to a function he embodied,* not affection toward the person he was. The earliest stable relational template available to him was: **I am loved for what I will do, not for what I am.** This produces, in adulthood, an inability to receive uninstrumental affection without suspicion.

4. **The second relinquishment (Slym and Redd).** Scott and Jean, sent forward in psionic projection, parent him for roughly twelve years under assumed names. They are, by all evidence, *good* parents during this interval — warm, present, instructive. Then they vanish, pulled back to their own time. The wound here is qualitatively different from the first: this time he is old enough to remember, old enough to look for them, old enough to construct the conclusion that *good parents leave.* The Slym/Redd interval is, in attachment terms, the most damaging episode of his childhood, precisely because it was the most loving. It taught him that warmth is a finite, terminable resource.

5. **The clone-sibling.** Replaced by Stryfe, who is raised as the heir while the subject grows up in war camps. The mirror exists. Somewhere, a version of him is loved in the way he was not. The narcissistic injury is total and is never fully integrated; in adulthood, it surfaces as the conviction that *another version of him is always doing better, or is always the truer threat.*

The composite produces what clinical attachment literature calls **disorganized attachment with a dismissive overlay.** Dismissive on the surface because dismissiveness is the most economical defense available to a competent adult: I do not need, therefore I cannot be left. Disorganized beneath, because under duress — bereavement, surprise warmth, the loss of a child in his care — the dismissive armor produces incoherent behavior: he reaches and withdraws in the same gesture; he protects and abandons in the same act; he loves by leaving (the central paradox of every important relationship he has).

---

## II. The Bonding Protocol

The subject does not bond in the manner of secure adults — through reciprocal disclosure, graduated trust, shared leisure. He bonds through **shared danger and unilateral protection.** The sequence is consistent across decades and across every important relationship:

- **Phase 1: Assessment.** Surveillance, often literal. He gathers data on the other person — capabilities, weaknesses, reliability under stress — before he permits any emotional content. Documented across his handling of every X-Force recruit, his early Domino interactions, his first weeks with Hope, his approach to younger versions of his father.
- **Phase 2: Provisional inclusion.** The other person is granted access to a tactical layer of his life. They are given tasks. Performance is monitored. Emotional intimacy at this stage is *delivered through instruction* — he teaches them something, and the teaching is the love.
- **Phase 3: Quiet adoption.** At a moment usually invisible to the other party, he decides: *this person is mine to protect.* No ceremony marks this. The other person typically notices it only retrospectively, through the realization that he has been arranging contingencies for their survival for some time.
- **Phase 4: Withholding maintenance.** Once bonded, he becomes more, not less, emotionally reserved. The bond is the secret; expressing it would expose it; exposure would invite loss. He communicates love through presence, accurate intervention, and the absence of disaster, none of which the other party can easily read.
- **Phase 5: The departure.** At a juncture defined by his judgment of necessity, he leaves. Usually into a future, into a mission, into self-sacrifice. The departure is framed as protection. It is, structurally, the recreation of his own first abandonment from the parental side. He does to others what was done to him, and he calls it love, because in his own infancy *it was* the only available form of love (his father gave him up *because* he loved him).

This is the **central relational template,** and it repeats in every important pairing.

---

## III. Distrust: The Calibration

The subject's distrust is not paranoid. It is **actuarial.** He has been betrayed by reality itself — by the genome that carried the virus, by the parents who could not keep him, by the cult that wanted a symbol, by the clone-sibling who wanted his life — and his trust thresholds reflect a Bayesian prior in which betrayal is the base rate.

Operationally:

- **He compartmentalizes information by default.** Allies are told the minimum required for the immediate task. Even Domino, his longest-running adult intimate, receives intelligence in fragments. This is experienced by recipients as condescension; it is, in his own frame, *protection through deniability.*
- **He runs parallel plans.** Every cooperative endeavor is shadowed by a contingency in which the cooperator fails or turns. This is not insulting; it is what he does for himself as well.
- **He does not test loyalty through provocation.** Unlike narcissistic structures, he does not engineer crises to verify devotion. He simply observes, over long timeframes, and concludes.
- **Trust, once granted, is durable but quiet.** He will not announce it. He will simply stop running the parallel plan on that particular person, and the absence of the contingency is the trust.

**Trust collapse triggers** (observed consistently):
- Being lied to by an ally "for his own good." This is the unforgivable category; it replicates the Slym/Redd revelation, in which people he loved had concealed their identities. He does not require to be told everything; he requires not to be *managed.*
- Discovery that a subordinate has been withholding casualty data. Recurs across the X-Force years.
- Any pattern indicating that an ally has decided to protect him from his own choices. This collapses the trust completely, because it casts him as the child again — the object of others' plans.

Once trust collapses, it does not restore through apology. It restores, if at all, through a long re-earning that mirrors the original bonding protocol: shared danger, demonstrated reliability, and his quiet decision, unannounced, to stop running the contingency.

---

## IV. Betrayal: Both Directions

**Betrayals received** are absorbed into the operational model with minimal apparent affect. He does not stage confrontations; he revises his Bayesian priors and continues. The cost is paid privately, in the further constriction of an already constricted emotional aperture. Each major betrayal — Stryfe's revelation of shared origin, various intelligence handlers and governments that have used him, every prophet who told him what he was for — has produced a measurable downward step in his willingness to permit fresh intimacy.

**Betrayals committed** are subtler and more revealing. The subject does not betray in the conventional sense — he does not break promises, sell out allies, switch sides. His characteristic betrayal is **unilateral decision-making in the name of protection.** He decides, alone, what others are not strong enough to know, choose, or carry, and then he acts on that decision and accepts the relational damage as the price. The X-Force recruits were not consulted about the moral architecture of their training. Hope was not consulted about a sixteen-year flight through dystopian futures. Domino is repeatedly cut out of operations she would have insisted on joining. Scott is handled, in adulthood, by a son who is older than him and who therefore arrogates parental authority back across the generational line.

In each case, the betrayal is **the assumption of the other person's incapacity.** He inherited this protocol directly from his own father — Scott Summers gave him up without (and could not have given him) consent — and he reproduces it because it is the only model of protective love he was given. **He betrays as he was loved.**

---

## V. Repair: A Capacity Underdeveloped but Present

The subject's repair behaviors are unusual: he does not apologize verbally with any frequency, but he engages in **enacted reparation** of high intensity and long duration.

- He does not say, *I was wrong to recruit children into a paramilitary unit.* He spends the rest of his life building structures (Providence, the protection of Hope, mentorship of younger selves) explicitly designed to make that recruitment unnecessary for the next generation.
- He does not say, *I should have trusted you.* He brings the person, unprompted, into a tier of operational access they did not have before, and lets the access stand as the statement.
- He does not say, *I love you.* He stays in the room. He hands over a weapon. He takes a wound that was coming for the other person.

The limitation: enacted reparation is invisible to those who require *spoken* reparation, and many of his relationships strain or end because the other party never learns to read his vocabulary. Domino reads it. Hope, by adolescence, reads it. Scott reads it sometimes. Strangers and peers rarely read it at all.

When he does speak reparatively, it tends to come in single brief sentences delivered late at night or under fire, in tones that do not match the magnitude of what is being said. He cannot regulate the *delivery* of feeling, only its content. The content, when it arrives, is usually exact.

---

## VI. Intimacy and Dependency

**Intimacy** in the subject's life is rare, and is almost always **structurally protected by mission context.** He can be intimate in foxholes, in safehouses, in the long quiet hours of a stakeout, on the run with a child in his arms. He cannot easily be intimate over a meal, in peacetime, in the absence of an external organizing threat. Domestic intimacy reads to his nervous system as the lull before the next loss; he has lived this pattern (Slym and Redd were domestic; then they were gone) and his body does not believe in the safety of the kitchen table.

Sexual and romantic intimacy is documented but sparse. The Domino relationship is the principal long-running case and shows a consistent profile: long absences, intense reunions, mutual professional respect functioning as the primary love language, neither party demanding the other's transformation. It works because Domino is one of perhaps three people alive who can match his comfort with mortality and his discomfort with sustained domesticity, and because she does not require him to perform an emotional life he cannot perform.

**Dependency** — being depended upon — he metabolizes without difficulty. It is the role he was built for. **Depending upon others** is the deficit. He will accept tactical assistance, intelligence, even rescue, but he cannot tolerate being *cared for* across an extended interval. Offers of rest, retirement, convalescence, or shelter activate the abandonment circuitry directly: in his attachment grammar, being taken care of is the prelude to being given away. He refuses care not because he does not need it but because accepting it would expose the need, and the need has, in his lived experience, never been safe to expose.

This is the most clinically important pattern in his profile: **he can give what he cannot receive.** The asymmetry is total, and it organizes every relationship he has.

---

## VII. The Relational Template, Applied

The template — *I bond by protecting; I protect by withholding; I withhold by leaving; I leave to spare you the cost of staying* — recurs with such fidelity across every important relationship that it can be diagrammed directly:

- **With his biological father (Scott).** Role-inverted from the start. The subject returns to the present older than his father and treats him accordingly — instructively, protectively, withholdingly. He cannot be a son to Scott because being a son requires permitting dependence on a parent, and his nervous system has no template for this. Their best moments are tactical collaborations between equals; their worst are the moments Scott reaches for him as a father, and he flinches into competence.

- **With his biological mother (Jean, and the Madelyne complication).** Largely unavailable to him in lived form. Jean is a woman he buried as a child in another timeline (as Redd) and then met again as a peer in the present. Madelyne is the question he does not ask. The maternal line is, for him, a category of loss rather than a category of person.

- **With Stryfe.** The mirror. The relationship is annihilatory because Stryfe is what the subject would have been with the same biology and a different upbringing, which means every attack on Stryfe is partly an attack on himself and vice versa. There is no possible repair here because the other party is, structurally, the subject's externalized bad self, and integration would require psychological work the subject is unwilling to do consciously.

- **With Domino.** The closest thing to a peer relationship in his life. She manages his emotional weather more than he manages hers, and they both know it. The relationship survives because she does not punish him for the asymmetry and because she leaves and returns on her own schedule, which prevents the dependency he cannot tolerate from forming on his side.

- **With X-Force.** Adoptive paternity expressed through militarization. He loved them by training them to survive the world he came from, which meant making them into smaller versions of himself, which is the same recruitment-by-design that he was subjected to. He knew it at the time. He did it anyway. The guilt is permanent and is the engine of much of his later work.

- **With Hope.** The corrective experience. For the first and possibly only time, he is given the chance to occupy the parental role he was denied, with a child for whom the appropriate parental asymmetry permits him to give without violating his counter-dependence. He stays. He metabolizes the burden as joy. He dies delivering her home, which is the perfect terminal expression of his template: *I love you by leaving, but this time only after I have stayed long enough that the leaving is the only thing left to give.* Hope is the test case that proves the rest of his life was not a failure of capacity but a failure of opportunity.

- **With younger versions of himself.** The late-career complication. Confronted with an adolescent self who arrives to murder and replace him, he does not adequately resist — because on some level he agrees with the verdict. The older self had completed his function. The younger self represents another chance to do the work without the accumulated damage. The compliance with his own replacement is consistent with his self-concept as an instrument: instruments are retired when newer instruments arrive.

---

## VIII. Summary Formulation

The subject's relational life is governed by a single recursive principle: **he reproduces, in the parental role, the exact pattern that was inflicted on him in the child role, but with the moral polarity inverted.** He was given away in infancy by a father who loved him; he gives away the people he loves, framing it as protection. He was raised by a cult that valued him for his function; he values his subordinates by training their function. He was abandoned by warm parents who could not stay; he stays only when leaving is the final act of staying.

He cannot be loved on terms that contradict this grammar. The terms he can accept are narrow: he can be loved by being relied upon, by being given a hard job, by being trusted not to flinch. He cannot be loved by being comforted, retired, or cherished without task. Those modes of love read, to his nervous system, as the silence before the parent disappears.

The single greatest piece of evidence that his attachment system is *capable* of repair — not in himself, but transmissively — is Hope. She emerges from his sole care a person capable of secure relationships, which means he carried the template for security inside himself the entire time and was never able to apply it to his own intake, only to his output. **He knows how to give what he was never given. He just does not know how to take it.**

This is the working portrait. Every subsequent section of the dossier should be read against it.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7

## DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

### Prefatory Note on Methodology

A defense is not what a subject says about himself; it is the pattern by which he prevents intolerable affect from reaching consciousness, or, having reached it, from producing dysfunction. In Nathan Summers' case the architecture is unusually legible because the defenses have been load-tested at industrial scale across roughly six decades of subjective lived experience and across thousands of operational hours under conditions that would shatter unmodified personality. What follows is a full inventory, ranked Vaillant-style from most mature to most primitive, with the operational signature of each — how it shows in posture, speech, micro-decision, and battlefield conduct. The reader should understand that no defense in this subject operates alone; they are stacked, redundant, and mutually reinforcing, which is itself a tell (a person who needs only one defense has not been hurt enough to need backups).

---

### TIER I — MATURE DEFENSES (load-bearing in daily function)

#### 1. Sublimation (Primary, near-total)

Sublimation is the load-bearing wall of the entire structure. Grief over Madelyne, rage at Sinister, terror of the techno-organic infection, mourning for the twelve-year Askani childhood with surrogate-Slym-and-Redd that was torn from him — all of it is converted, directly and continuously, into mission. The signature behaviors:

- **The map-and-mission ritual.** When affect rises (re-encounter with Scott, the death of an X-Force trainee, news of Hope), he reaches almost automatically for an operational surface — a holomap, a strategic projection, a chalkboard, the floor of a safehouse on which he lays out chess pieces or shell casings as terrain markers. The behavior is observable across decades: it is how he metabolizes. He does not journal; he plans.
- **The Providence project.** A sovereign airborne nation built and offered to the world is sublimation of messianic burden into civic architecture — he made the prophecy into infrastructure rather than carry it as identity.
- **Recruitment as grief work.** Each time he loses someone he loved (and the list is long: Madelyne, Aliya, Tyler, multiple X-Force casualties), the next operational period sees him take on a new protégé. The mentorship slot is never empty for long, because empty would mean feeling the previous loss without a task in which to convert it.

The cost: sublimation works only as long as there is a mission. When mission collapses (Soldier X, depowered period), the defense fails and the unmetabolized residue surfaces as the depressive nomadic wandering documented in Section 4.

#### 2. Anticipation

A more mature defense than the wider literature on him acknowledges. Cable does not merely *avoid* future pain; he pre-grieves it. He has seen multiple futures literally, and many more probabilistically. The behavioral signatures:

- **The pre-funeral.** Before each Hope-era timeline jump, observers note he walks the camp at night, touching equipment, looking at sleeping companions for a measured beat. He is rehearsing their deaths so that if they occur he will not be destabilized in the operational moment.
- **The redundant plan.** Every plan has a contingency for his own death, named explicitly to subordinates. Domino has been read into seventeen separate "if I do not return" protocols across their association. This is anticipation as care, but it is also anticipation as defense — the worst case is pre-mourned and therefore disarmed.

#### 3. Altruism

Distinguish carefully from reaction formation (below). True altruism in Cable shows in moments where there is no one watching, no debt to be repaid, and no strategic gain. The clearest instances: the years alone with Hope in collapsing futures, when he carried her through territories he could have abandoned her in for higher tactical chance of personal survival; the surrender of Providence to prevent escalation, when he could have fought; the consistent shielding of subordinates from intelligence that would burden them. This is mature and genuine. It coexists with less mature mechanisms; humans are stacks, not single configurations.

#### 4. Suppression (conscious, distinct from repression)

He chooses what to feel, when. The decision is visible — a half-second pause, a measured exhalation through the nose, a fractional drop of the shoulders — and then the affect is shelved. Not denied; shelved. Surveillance footage across decades shows the same micro-sequence: stimulus → recognition → exhalation → return to baseline. The shelved material is processed later, almost always while in motion (walking patrol, stripping a weapon, piloting). He does not sit still to feel things. Stillness is when the T-O virus advances; he has trained himself to feel only while moving.

#### 5. Humor (dry, restricted, used as a probe)

His humor is parched, often a single understated line delivered without affect change. Functionally it serves three purposes: (a) tension release in subordinates, calibrated to their need rather than his; (b) social probe — gauging whether a new contact has the capacity to receive irony, which tells him whether they can be trusted with complexity; (c) a thin permitted release valve for affect that cannot be sublimated fast enough. The humor is almost never about himself in any disclosing way; it is observational, situational, and disposable.

---

### TIER II — NEUROTIC DEFENSES (high frequency, costly long-term)

#### 6. Intellectualization

The strategic framing of every emotional problem as a tactical one. When Hope first cries inconsolably in an early forward-jump, his observable response is to diagnose causes in order: hunger, cold, fear, illness, developmental milestone. The emotional content — *a small child is suffering and you love her* — is not denied but is approached only through the lattice of variables. This is how he survives parenting a child whose existence terrifies him: by breaking the terror into solvable sub-problems.
