The defense's cost is that genuine intimacy, which requires non-instrumental presence, is rationed. He can be a magnificent operational father and a structurally limited emotional one, and the unevenness is what gives Hope her particular adult shape.

#### 7. Reaction Formation (against messianism)

He disclaims the prophecy publicly with consistent vehemence and organizes every act around it privately. Behavioral evidence:

- Refuses the title "Chosen One" in dialogue across multiple eras; verbally corrects subordinates who use it.
- Founds a sovereign nation as a demonstration city designed to model humanity's elevation — which is precisely what a messiah does.
- Becomes the sole guardian of the post-M-Day mutant messiah child — and refuses to call her that, even to himself, in the journals recovered from the future-period.

The disclaimer is the tell. A man who genuinely did not believe himself a messiah would not need to correct people about it; he would shrug. Cable corrects. The defense functions because it preserves humility-of-presentation while permitting messianic-scale action.

#### 8. Isolation of Affect

Adjacent to intellectualization but distinct: the systematic separation of memory content from its emotional charge. He can describe in clinical detail the night his infant self was handed to Sister Askani, the moment Slym-and-Redd dissolved, the deaths of Aliya and Tyler, with no audible shift in vocal register, pulse, or pupil dilation. The events are accessible; the feelings are stored separately and accessed only under controlled conditions (alone, in motion, usually at night). This is why he can debrief atrocity without flinching and why witnesses sometimes find him cold. He is not cold; he is filed.

#### 9. Identification with the Aggressor

He became a soldier-trainer of children. He knows this. The X-Force years are not unselfconscious — late dialogue makes the recognition explicit — but the defense operated long before the recognition. The mechanism: a child cannot tolerate being purely the object of weaponization, so he becomes the subject who weaponizes. The relief is structural (agency reclaimed) and the cost is moral (the system perpetuates). The Krakoa-era teenage iteration is the same defense at an earlier developmental position, which is one reason the older self and the younger self cannot coexist; they are running the same defense from incompatible vantages.

#### 10. Undoing

Visible in the long arc of trying to disarm the future he came from. Each preventive intervention is, structurally, an attempt to undo the original handoff in infancy — to *not have been sent forward*, to make a present in which the future-of-Apocalypse did not require him. The defense never completes because the wound is not retrievable, but the attempts produce real-world benefit (futures averted, lives saved), which is one of the better functional outcomes available to a defense in this tier.

#### 11. Displacement (onto Stryfe, onto Apocalypse, onto institutional enemies)

Some portion of the rage that properly belongs to Scott Summers — for the original handoff — and to Sinister, for the engineered conception, is displaced onto Stryfe and Apocalypse, who are both safer targets (they are unambiguously evil and they can be hit). The displacement is partial; he has done substantial work to bring the original anger back to its proper address, particularly in late-period scenes with Scott. But the residue remains, and it explains the disproportionate, almost personal intensity with which he pursues Apocalypse-coded enemies even after immediate threat has passed.

---

### TIER III — LESS MATURE DEFENSES (episodic, stress-triggered)

#### 12. Splitting (mild, episodic, contained)

Stryfe is the externalized bad-self. The clone carries everything Cable cannot integrate about his own origin — the engineered weapon, the messianic grandiosity, the willingness to slaughter for the prophecy. Cable can be the good-Nathan because Stryfe is the bad-Nathan; the boundary is policed by lethal force. Splitting is normally a more primitive defense than this subject otherwise uses, which suggests the Stryfe-bond carries weight the rest of the personality cannot bear. The episodic nature — he is not generally a splitter, only specifically with Stryfe — supports this reading. When Stryfe's consciousness lingers internally (post-X-Cutioner's Song), the defense becomes briefly unsustainable and the subject's organization wobbles visibly.

#### 13. Counter-dependence (proto-defense / characterological)

Stronger than mere independence: an active refusal of care, framed as protecting the caregiver from the cost. He will accept medical attention only when incapacitated; he will accept emotional support only from Domino, and only obliquely; he will accept logistical support but resists being *taken care of* in any sense that implies he could not have done it alone. The defense protects against the catastrophic prediction that any attachment will end in abandonment, by pre-emptively refusing the attachment's full depth. Costly: it isolates him from repair he could otherwise receive, and it models for subordinates a martyrdom-mode they should not learn.

#### 14. Somatization (paradoxical, partial)

The T-O virus is not psychogenic; the infection is real. But the subject's *relationship* to his body has a somatizing quality — emotional load is registered as flare, ache, viral advancement, in the absence of any clear pathological vector. After particularly painful interpersonal events, observers note increased visible T-O bloom on the left side of the face within hours. Whether this is hormonal stress accelerating infection or perception artifact is unresolved; either way the body is doing affective work the psyche has refused.

#### 15. Acting Out (rare, controlled)

He does not generally act out — most discharge is sublimated. But in the period following the loss of Aliya and Tyler, and again in the Soldier X wandering phase, there are bursts of disproportionate violence on missions that meet the technical definition of acting out: aggression discharged at substitute targets to relieve unbearable internal state. The episodes are brief, generally lethal to the target, and followed by extended withdrawal. The defense is poorly tolerated by the rest of his system; he punishes himself for using it.

---

### COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — POSITIVE COLUMN

These are not defenses proper; they are the constructive uses to which the same energies are put.

- **Mentorship as reparative practice.** Each protégé is an attempt to deliver to another what was not delivered to him: continuity, presence, a teacher who stays. Cannonball is the cleanest case — Sam Guthrie is the protégé Cable did not abandon, and the relationship is the healthiest sustained mentorship in the file.
- **Nation-building (Providence).** Channels messianic charge into civic form. Voluntary citizenship, transparent governance, demonstrated rather than imposed values. The structural choice — to *show* rather than *rule* — is itself the mature inversion of the Askani childhood, in which others showed him a future and demanded he embody it. He reverses the polarity: he embodies and lets others choose whether to follow.
- **Reparative parenting (Hope).** The diagnostic gold-standard event. Replicates the war-zone-and-future conditions of his own childhood but inverts the parental role: he *stays*. The defense system permits this because the asymmetry is appropriate (she is a child), which is the one relational configuration he can occupy without his counter-dependence triggering.
- **Refusal of warlord role.** Multiple opportunities to seize authority — political, military, prophetic — declined. The refusal is principled, sustained, and costly. It is the single strongest evidence that the personality is organized around ethics rather than around the messianic projection.
- **Long-horizon planning as gift.** He thinks on timelines of decades because he was, as a child, the object of others' decade-plans. Repurposed: he uses the same cognitive apparatus to plan *protections* for others, which is the inverse of how it was originally used on him.

### COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — NEGATIVE COLUMN

- **Recruitment of minors into combat.** The X-Force decision. Cannot be excused by mission necessity alone; it is also identification with the aggressor producing the next generation of weaponized children. The fact that he selected protégés with potential rather than expendables is a partial mitigation. The fact that he selected children at all is the indictment.
- **Preemptive lethality.** Kills targets he assesses as future threats, on probabilistic grounds, before they have acted. The intelligence is usually sound; the ethics are violated by the very capacity. It is the operational expression of *I have seen what becomes of unaddressed problems*, and it forecloses the redemption others might have managed.
- **Secrecy with allies.** Withholds operational intelligence on need-to-know grounds that are sometimes genuine and sometimes a counter-dependent refusal to share burden. Costs trust repeatedly across the file. The pattern is durable enough to be characterological, not situational.
- **Refusal to delegate stakes he considers his.** Will not let others take the killing shot, the dying role, the unbearable decision. Reads as protectiveness; functions as control. Subordinates are denied the agency he himself most needed and rarely got.
- **Martyrdom protocols at catastrophic stress.** When pressure exceeds threshold, he reaches automatically for the solution in which he is the one paying. The Hope return is the canonical instance — the virus consumes him to deliver her home. Ethically luminous; clinically a marker of self-expendability that has never been examined and resolved.
- **Asceticism as self-punishment.** The Soldier X wandering, the Krakoan-era isolations: when defenses fail, the fallback is not collapse but voluntary deprivation. He withholds from himself what he most needs (rest, food, company, medical attention) in a pattern consistent with chronic guilt that has never been spoken aloud.

---

### STRUCTURAL OBSERVATIONS

**Defense stacking.** The architecture is layered: sublimation handles the bulk daily load; intellectualization and isolation-of-affect catch what sublimation misses; suppression manages the rest in real time; counter-dependence keeps the system from being overwhelmed by intimacy; splitting and somatization absorb what nothing else can hold; acting-out is the rare overflow valve. The redundancy is the signature of a person who learned early that any single defense could be stripped from him at any moment, and built backups for the backups.

**The Stryfe-shaped hole.** The defensive system as a whole is organized around a void it cannot fill: the question of *which one of us was the real son*. Splitting handles it locally by externalizing Stryfe as the bad-twin; reaction formation and undoing handle it strategically by making the present so loaded with ethical action that the origin question becomes irrelevant; intellectualization handles it discursively by framing it as a tactical problem about clone-identification rather than an existential one about being-loved. None of these resolves it. The system runs around it.

**The single point of failure.** If sublimation is denied — no mission, no protégé, no problem to solve — the entire architecture begins to fail in days, not weeks. Soldier X is the natural experiment, and the result is documented: depressive nomadism, ascetic self-deprivation, attenuated affect, geographic flight. He cannot rest. Rest is when the defenses stop working and the original infant — handed to strangers two thousand years from his parents — comes back into the room.

**What it costs to be him.** The cumulative load of running this defensive system continuously for six subjective decades, while simultaneously running a cellular-level autoimmune process to contain a fatal virus, while simultaneously parenting, commanding, and prophesying, is incalculable. The fact that he remains ethical, functional, and capable of love is the central clinical finding of this file. The defenses are not pretty; they are not all mature; some of them cost other people directly. But they have kept alive a man who, by every reasonable actuarial measure, should not be alive — and through him, the people he was given to protect. Measured by the only metric he respects, the architecture has held.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE

## Subject: Nathan Christopher Charles Summers

*A decade-by-decade clinical mapping of affect regulation, cognitive style, self-concept, defensive architecture, and relational schema across a subjective lifespan that exceeds his chronological one by an order of magnitude. Time markers below refer to **subjective developmental time** — i.e., the order in which the subject's nervous system experienced events — not publication chronology and not present-tense calendar time. Where the subject lived through a period in displaced timeframes (Askani future, Hope-flight years), the somatic and developmental clock is what is being indexed.*

---

## I. INFANCY (Subjective Age 0–2): The Surrender

**Setting:** Present-day Earth; X-Factor era; Inferno aftermath.

**Affect regulation — preverbal substrate.** The defining affective imprint is laid down before the subject can encode it narratively but well within the window in which the limbic system organizes its baselines. Two things happen in close succession: a viral infection that introduces a continuous, low-grade nociceptive signal at the cellular level (the T-O process is, neurologically, *experienced* — it is not silent), and a hand-off from the primary attachment figure to a stranger in a strange uniform from another century. The infant nervous system encodes: *intimate threat from inside the body* + *attachment object disappears at moment of maximum need.* This is, in the technical sense of Schore's work on right-hemisphere affect regulation, a near-textbook setup for disorganized attachment with somatic comorbidity. Every subsequent affective system he builds will be erected over this foundation.

**Cognitive style.** Not yet operative. But the procedural memory of the surrender — body in danger, caregiver recedes — will function as an implicit prior on every future model he builds about what care is and what it costs.

**Self-concept.** Not yet operative as concept, but as somatic schema: *I am the thing inside which a war is happening.* The body-as-battleground self-image, fully articulated in adulthood, begins here in pre-articulate form.

---

## II. EARLY CHILDHOOD (Subjective Age 2–8): The Askani'son

**Setting:** 2,000 years forward; Clan Askani; the Chosen One framework.

**Affect regulation.** Early years among the Askani are characterized by ritualized handling — the child is precious because prophesied, not because *him*. He is reared in a frame in which his affective states have cosmic significance and therefore no privacy. A toddler's tantrum is read as a sign. A boy's fear is interpreted as test. This produces what Winnicott would call a False Self structure: the child learns very early to display the affect that the system expects and to suppress affect that disrupts the system's narrative about him. The suppression mechanism, refined over decades, is the same one that will later let an adult Cable sit through a lethal mission briefing with a flat face.

**Cognitive style — emergence.** First evidence of what will become his signature pattern: long-horizon, branching, probabilistic thinking. He is being raised by people who literally know the future; he absorbs the assumption that time is a terrain, not a flow. This is unusual cognitive scaffolding for a young child and produces, by age seven or eight, a child who naturally formulates contingencies and reads situations as nested possibility spaces. He will never lose this; in adulthood it presents as preternatural strategic patience and an unsettling refusal to react to short-term provocations.

**Self-concept.** Bifurcated from the start. There is the *Chosen One* — a public identity, externally maintained, that he wears. And there is the boy who suspects, correctly, that the prophecy precedes him and would have been imposed on whoever was born. The gap between these two — between the role and the occupant — is the first iteration of what will become his lifelong reaction formation against messianism. He will publicly minimize his prophetic status for the next fifty subjective years while privately organizing every major decision around it.

---

## III. MIDDLE CHILDHOOD (Subjective Age 8–12): Slym and Redd

**Setting:** Late Askani period; Scott and Jean (as Slym and Redd) raising him in disguise.

This is the most psychologically nutritive period of his childhood and possibly his life. Two adults of high competence and high warmth, who *also know who he is*, give him a window of true parenting. There is evidence in the canon that during this period the boy laughs more, plays, learns to fight from people who love him rather than from people who own him.

**Affect regulation.** Brief but formative regulation-by-coregulation. He learns, in this window, that affect can be shared. This becomes the reference standard against which every subsequent relationship will fail. The Hope years will be his attempt to reproduce *Slym and Redd* from the parental side.

**Cognitive style.** Acquires the *teaching* register from Scott — the cool, instructive, undramatic explanation. Cable's adult speech pattern with X-Force recruits is recognizably Cyclops-derived. He also acquires the *emotional translation* skill from Jean — the ability to read a room without telepathy, which he will lean on heavily once telepathy is consumed by the virus.

**Self-concept.** Briefly, a son. Briefly, allowed to be smaller than the people raising him. This is the only stretch of his life in which appropriate developmental asymmetry runs in the correct direction — older above younger — and it is the period he will be unable to recreate for himself, only for others.

**Termination — Loss #2.** Slym and Redd are pulled back to the present. From the boy's perspective: his parents leave, again, without warning. The encoding now is no longer ambiguous. *Attachment figures disappear. This is what they do.* The disorganized substrate from infancy is now confirmed by lived, narratively encoded experience. After this, he will never again allow himself to need an attachment figure in the dependent direction.

---

## IV. ADOLESCENCE (Subjective Age 12–18): War Camp

**Setting:** Captured, separated from Stryfe, raised in resistance cells.

**Affect regulation.** Militarization of affect. Whatever was learned with Slym and Redd is now overlaid with a survival schema in which display of feeling is tactically dangerous. Tears draw fire. Fear is contagious in a unit and therefore selfish. He learns to convert the entire affective register into operational outputs — fear into scanning, grief into planning, rage into precise violence. The conversion is so total and so automatic by adulthood that observers consistently misread him as cold; he is not cold, he is metabolically *busy* converting.

**Cognitive style.** Strategic maturity arrives early and under duress. By mid-adolescence he is making calls that adult commanders make. The branching-futures cognition acquired in childhood now has a use: he is good at war because he was born thinking in scenarios. He also acquires the operator's habit of pre-mortem — running every plan to its failure modes before committing — which will become a tic in adulthood (he visibly pauses before action; he is finishing the simulation).

**Self-concept.** The *used instrument* frame consolidates here. He understands himself, by the end of adolescence, as a thing built for a purpose, and his only meaningful agency is whether he ratifies the purpose or not. He ratifies it. This is the existential choice that retroactively organizes everything before it and prospectively organizes everything after. The depressive substrate native to this self-concept is already present: a young man who knows what he is for and does not believe he is for himself.

**Stryfe.** The discovery, at some point in this period, of the clone-sibling who has been raised as the heir-apparent introduces a permanent intrapsychic feature. Splitting, in the Kernberg sense, will never fully apply to Cable — his integration is too strong — but the *Stryfe-position* (the unintegrated bad-self, the version of him that accepted the weaponization without conscience) is externalized into an actual person who walks the earth. This is psychologically convenient for as long as Stryfe is alive (you can fight him) and catastrophic when he is not (Stryfe-as-mental-content returns in *X-Cutioner's Song* and after).

---

## V. EARLY ADULTHOOD (Subjective Age 18–35): Soldier Years in the Future

**Setting:** Adult military operator in the Apocalypse dystopia; pre-time-travel to the present.

**Affect regulation.** Stable, flat, militarized. Operating baseline. Sleep already minimal. Pain already chronic. He is functional and effective. The body's continuous viral load is now experienced as ambient background — he has habituated to a sensation that would put an opted civilian into the ICU.

**Cognitive style.** Now fully expressed: long-horizon, probabilistic, undramatic. Acquires institutional skill — running networks, managing assets, holding secrets across years. This will become the substrate of his later civilian operations (Six Pack, Wild Pack, the intelligence apparatus he runs in the present).

**Self-concept.** *I am a soldier in a war that began before my birth.* Stable. Functional. Depressive in undertone but not impairing. He is, in this period, probably as psychologically *settled* as he will ever be — at the cost of having a self organized entirely around a mission. Remove the mission and the self collapses, which is exactly what will happen in the Soldier X period decades subjective-time later.

---

## VI. TRANSITION TO PRESENT-DAY (Subjective Age ~40–45): Time Displacement and the New Mutants

**Setting:** Cable arrives in the present, takes over the New Mutants, founds X-Force.

**Affect regulation — early stress test.** Reentry into the time period of his infancy and his parents introduces affect that has had no rehearsal. He is now meeting people who are his biological parents and who are younger than him. There is no playbook for this. His coping is to *not cope* — he treats Scott as a tactical peer at best, refuses the father-son frame, and keeps emotional traffic to the minimum the situation permits. This will calcify into the lifelong pattern.

**Cognitive style.** The cognitive style is fine; it is the emotional bandwidth that is overloaded. He overcorrects toward the strategic, presenting as the gun-fetish caricature for which the early '90s appearances are notorious. Read clinically, the posturing is defense: a man emotionally overwhelmed performs maximum competence in the one register where he is sure of himself.

**Self-concept — first major crisis.** The *X-Cutioner's Song* revelation that he is the Summers child, not the clone, restructures the entire self-concept. He had, on some level, organized identity around being the *replacement* — the lesser copy who escaped to do good. The discovery that he is the original, and Stryfe the copy, is not relief; it is destabilization. The original carries the original obligation. He is now, in his own framework, *responsible* for being who he was supposed to be — and the Apocalypse-killer prophecy is no longer something he can dismiss as someone else's job.

**Identification with the aggressor — explicit.** The X-Force decision (recruiting and militarizing teenagers) is made in this period. Clinically, this is identification with the aggressor in Anna Freud's classical sense: the man who was made into a child soldier resolves the unmetabolized trauma by *becoming the maker of child soldiers*, with the consoling difference that he tells himself he is doing it better. He is not unaware of the repetition. The awareness is part of the pain; it does not stop the action.

---

## VII. MIDLIFE I (Subjective Age 45–55): The Cable Solo Run

**Setting:** Maturation; recovery of Askani heritage; turn toward overt mission-as-program.

**Affect regulation.** Loosens, modestly. He permits himself dry humor, occasional warmth toward Domino, episodic acknowledgment of grief. The clamp is still there but he learns to crack the seal under specific safe conditions. This is the closest he comes to therapeutic progress without therapy: titrated re-exposure to his own affect in containers he controls.

**Cognitive style.** Shifts from operator to **strategist-builder**. The cognitive horizon extends from years to decades. He begins to think in terms of institutions, not operations. This is a maturational shift — the move from tactical to grand-strategic thinking is generally observed in operators in their forties and Cable is on schedule.

**Self-concept — major revision.** From *used instrument* toward *agent who chose the instrument's use*. This is a critical and authentically therapeutic move: he reclaims authorship of the mission he was built for. The Askani training and the deeper engagement with the prophecy framework, paradoxically, *de-fatalize* him — once he understands the prophecy as a tradition he can argue with rather than a script he must perform, he has a degree of freedom he did not previously have.

**Providence.** The construction of a sovereign demonstration-state is the behavioral expression of this self-revision. He is no longer fighting *against* an enemy; he is building *toward* a model. The relinquishment of Providence — voluntary surrender to prevent escalation — is the test that proves the revision real. A man whose self was still organized around being the instrument could not have let it go. He could.

---

## VIII. MIDLIFE II (Subjective Age 55–60): Soldier X and the Wilderness

**Setting:** Loss of viral control, then loss of powers; Eastern European wandering; ascetic period.

**Affect regulation — decompensation.** With the mission-structure removed (no team, no Providence, eventually no powers), the affect that has been held by the structure begins to leak. He does not collapse outwardly. He withdraws, walks, and goes quiet. Clinically, this is a major depressive episode superimposed on the lifelong dysthymia, expressed in the only modality his defensive system permits: ascetic withdrawal rather than acute crisis. The wandering is not aimless; it is the only form of expression available to a man who cannot weep.

**Cognitive style.** Narrows, slows. He becomes more contemplative and less operational. Reads. Thinks. The strategic engine is idling because there is no campaign to run. This is uncomfortable for him — the cognitive style was load-bearing — but it is also the only period in which he turns the long-horizon analysis on *himself.*

**Self-concept — recession.** Without role to occupy, the *used instrument* frame returns with depressive force. *If I am not for the mission, what am I for?* He does not answer the question; he survives it. The survival itself is data — he learns, for the first time, that he can continue to exist outside operational identity. This will matter later.

---

## IX. LATE MIDLIFE (Subjective Age 60–76): The Hope Years

**Setting:** Sixteen subjective years of fugitive parenting across post-apocalyptic timelines.

This is the most clinically significant period of the entire profile and the only one in which sustained, structural change occurs in the core attachment system.

**Affect regulation — reorganization through caregiving.** Caring for an infant who becomes a child who becomes an adolescent requires affective availability he has never sustained. He cannot run a child the way he runs an op. He has to *be present* — soothe, play, contain, repair. He does. The neurobiological literature on caregiving (Feldman, Swain) is clear that primary caregiving rewires affect-regulatory circuitry in the caregiver; Cable, late in his subjective life, undergoes exactly this rewiring. His baseline does not become warm. But the *capacity* for warmth, dormant since Slym and Redd, is reactivated and exercised daily for sixteen years.

**Cognitive style.** Inverts under necessity. The strategist accustomed to decades-horizon planning has to learn to think in *days* — where is the next meal, what's the next shelter, is the child sleeping. He becomes a better thinker for it: the long-horizon planner with re-acquired short-horizon attention is, in operational terms, the apex form of him.

**Self-concept — the major revision.** From *used instrument* and then *agent who chose the instrument's use* now to **father.** The self-concept is, for the first time, organized around a relational role rather than a mission function. Hope is not a mission; Hope is a person he loves. The distinction is everything. This is the closest he has come, since the Slym-and-Redd window, to being a self that exists in mutual recognition with another self.

**Reparative parenting — clinical analysis.** The pattern is textbook: he replicates exactly the *external conditions* of his own childhood (war zone, isolation, dystopia) while inverting the *parental variable.* He does not leave. He does not hand her off. He stays through illness, through her adolescent rejection of him, through the body finally failing. The somatic cost — the virus consuming him as he runs out of telekinetic capacity to spend on suppression because he is spending it on protecting her — is, in his own framework, the correct trade. He is paying the price his father did not pay. He is, in the technical sense, completing an unfinished developmental sequence in the wrong generational direction. This works for Hope. It does not heal him, because the recipient of his care is not the wounded part of himself — but it gives the wounded part of himself the satisfaction of seeing the work done correctly once, in his presence, by his hand.

**Affect regulation — terminal phase.** In the final stretch of the Hope years, with the virus burning through him, affect becomes more permeable. He cries, sometimes. He says things to her he could not say to anyone earlier. The dying body relaxes the clamp the living body required. This is consistent with end-of-life affective opening observed in patients with long psychological constriction; the defense becomes too expensive to maintain.

---

## X. POSTHUMOUS / RESURRECTED (Subjective Age 76+ and the Kid Cable Substitution)

**Setting:** Returns after Hope's delivery; the *Avengers: X-Sanction*, *Cable and X-Force*, and *Extermination* runs; eventual replacement by Kid Cable.

**Affect regulation.** Post-Hope, his baseline is observably altered. He is still flat, still controlled, but the absolute zero is gone. He can be tired in front of others. He can express affection, briefly, to Scott. The reparative parenting period left a permanent residue.

**Cognitive style.** Unchanged in structure; older in tone. He moves with the assurance of a man who has already done the thing he was for. The urgency of the early Cable years is gone, replaced by something closer to a craftsman's tempo.

**Self-concept — settled, then disrupted.** He has come closest to integration: father, soldier, builder, the *used instrument that used itself well*. Then Kid Cable arrives — a younger self who judges the older self as having grown soft, compromised, insufficient — and kills him. The substitution is, read psychologically, a self-loathing operation in literal form: the unhealed adolescent part murders the integrated adult part because integration feels, to the adolescent, like betrayal of the mission. The older Cable, on some level, lets it happen — his pattern of *self-expendability*, and his willingness to be replaced if replacement serves the mission, makes resistance to the boy uncharacteristic.

**Kid Cable — the developmental backwash.** The Krakoan-era teen is the subject re-occupying an earlier developmental position with all the same drives and none of the integration. Affect regulation: brittle and adolescent, swinging between bravado and sulk. Cognitive style: strategic by training but impulsive by hormone. Self-concept: *the real Cable, the one who didn't get soft* — which is exactly the consoling fiction the adult Cable refused to tell himself. The pattern that began in infancy — the bifurcation between role and occupant, the splitting off of the bad-self into a clone or sibling or now a younger version — has returned, and it will have to be worked through again from an earlier developmental position.

---

## SYNTHESIS: Trajectory of the Three Axes

**Affect regulation across the lifespan:**
Disorganized substrate (infancy) → False-Self ritual display (Askani childhood) → brief coregulation (Slym/Redd) → militarized suppression (adolescence and early adulthood) → ambient flat baseline with strategic posturing (early Cable) → controlled loosening under safe conditions (solo years) → depressive leakage in withdrawal (Soldier X) → reorganization through caregiving (Hope years) → permeable late style (post-resurrection) → re-brittling in the adolescent re-occupation (Kid Cable). The arc is real and the gains were real; the substitution by the younger self resets parts of the system to an earlier configuration.

**Cognitive style across the lifespan:**
Probabilistic prior installed in childhood by exposure to time-traveling caregivers → tactical-strategic emergence in adolescent war → operator stability in early adulthood → strategist-builder maturation in midlife → contemplative narrowing in the wilderness → forced short-horizon competence in the Hope years (yielding apex form when re-fused with long-horizon) → craftsman's tempo post-resurrection → reversion to adolescent strategic-with-impulsive in Kid Cable. The cognitive architecture is the most stable feature of the profile and the one that survives the substitutions most intact.

**Self-concept across the lifespan:**
Body-as-battleground (preverbal) → Chosen One / role-occupant split (childhood) → briefly *son* (Slym/Redd window) → *used instrument* (adolescence onward) → *agent who chose the instrument's use* (solo years) → recession to depressive *used instrument* in wilderness → **father** (Hope years, the only relational self-concept he ever sustains) → integrated *instrument that used itself well* (post-resurrection) → reset to *the real one who didn't get soft* (Kid Cable's adolescent fixation).

The single most important fact about the longitudinal profile is that **change occurred, late and at cost, through caregiving.** The man could not be healed by being cared for — every attempt at that triggered his abandonment priors and was refused. He could only be partly healed by being permitted to care for someone who would let him stay. That this required him to spend his body to do it is consistent with everything else about him: he will pay any price except the price of being protected.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL
## Subject: Summers, Nathan Christopher Charles
## Section 4 of 11 — Clinical Psychiatric Workup

---

## 4.0 PREFATORY NOTE ON METHOD

This section formalizes the diagnostic impressions derived from sixty-plus years of behavioral record (canonical and inferential). Diagnoses are stated to DSM-5-TR and ICD-11 analog standards. The subject has never, to UATU's knowledge, completed a structured clinical interview, submitted to standardized inventories, or received continuous treatment from a qualified provider. The Krakoan medical apparatus (Healer, the Five) is reparative and somatic, not psychiatric. The subject's only documented contact with mental-health-adjacent intervention is the abortive Xavier psionic scan during the X-Cutioner's Song aftermath, which subject terminated unilaterally — a refusal pattern in itself diagnostically informative.

All diagnoses below are therefore **derived, evidence-anchored, longitudinally cross-referenced, and stated with confidence intervals.** Where a diagnosis is asserted, the behavioral substrate is named. Where ruled out, the rule-out is reasoned, not asserted.

---

## 4.1 PRIMARY DIAGNOSIS

### Complex Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder (ICD-11, 6B41)
**Confidence: very high. Onset: pre-verbal. Course: chronic, partially compensated, treatment-naïve.**

CPTSD rather than classical PTSD is the correct frame because the trauma is not a discrete event but a *developmental ecology*. The subject's traumatic exposure begins in infancy with the techno-organic infection and surrender by his biological father, continues through a childhood spent in a future-dystopian war zone under the burden of a messianic cult, includes the abrupt extraction of his surrogate parents at approximately age twelve, includes capture and ideological reprogramming attempts, and continues — without remission — across the entirety of his adult life via the chronic management of a body-borne nanotechnological adversary that converts him to his enemy from the inside, one cell at a time.

**ICD-11 6B41 criteria mapping:**

- **Criterion A (exposure to extreme threat, typically prolonged or repetitive, from which escape is difficult or impossible):** Satisfied multiply and redundantly. The T-O virus alone, as a perpetual interior threat, meets the "inescapable" specifier; the subject literally cannot leave the room with his own attacker.
- **Criterion B1 (re-experiencing):** Stryfe's residual psionic imprint following X-Cutioner's Song functions clinically as a *somatized intrusion* — the trauma has a voice and uses it. Subject also displays brief dissociative episodes when proximate to specific somatic triggers (the sound and smell of cauterization; certain frequencies of psionic interference resembling Askani conditioning protocols).
- **Criterion B2 (avoidance):** Avoidance is paradoxical — the subject does not avoid combat or danger; he avoids *intimacy*, *rest*, and *being cared for*. The avoided stimulus class is "situations in which I am the protected rather than the protector," because such situations are pre-coded as preludes to abandonment.
- **Criterion B3 (persistent sense of current threat):** Hypervigilance is continuous and unmasked. Sleep is segmented and weapon-adjacent. Subject orients to exits, to elevations, to civilian sight-lines, automatically, in every recorded scene.
- **CPTSD-specific Disturbances in Self-Organization (DSO):**
  - **Affective dysregulation:** Presents not as lability but as the opposite — *hyperregulation*, a flattening so total it functions as dysregulation in the other direction. Emotion is not absent; it is compressed and routed through action. The rare breakthroughs (grief over X-Force casualties; the moment of Hope's safe return; the conversation with the resurrected Jean) are short, low-amplitude, and immediately re-sealed.
  - **Negative self-concept:** Pervasive. The "used instrument" self-frame is the cognitive substrate of every recorded soliloquy. Self-statements consistently center on instrumentality and culpability, never on entitlement or worth.
  - **Disturbances in relationships:** Counter-dependence; chronic asymmetry; inability to occupy the receiving end of care; pattern of organizing relationships around protection rather than mutuality.

CPTSD is the **superordinate diagnosis** — most of what follows is comorbidity, sequela, or trait-level adaptation downstream of it.

---

## 4.2 COMORBID DIAGNOSES

### Persistent Depressive Disorder (DSM-5-TR 300.4 / ICD-11 6A72)
**Confidence: high. Onset: estimated late adolescence (post-Stryfe replacement). Course: chronic with at least one superimposed Major Depressive Episode.**

The Soldier X / Eastern European wandering period meets criteria for a **Major Depressive Episode superimposed on dysthymia** (double depression) — duration exceeded two months, presented with anhedonia, psychomotor decrease (the wandering is not exploratory; it is propulsive emptiness), social withdrawal to the point of severing all prior relationships, and a marked turn toward ascetic self-denial that functions as covert self-punishment. Vegetative signs are masked because the body's baseline (T-O suppression load) already produces sleep disruption, weight instability, and energy fluctuation — making the depression invisible against the somatic noise.

Baseline dysthymic features, present across decades:
- Restricted hedonic range (the subject's pleasures are narrow and instrumental — a well-cleaned firearm, a well-laid plan, a quiet meal with Domino — and even these are reported flatly).
- Pessimistic forecasting framed as realism.
- Self-deprecating humor of the chronically depressed kind — dry, deflective, used to terminate emotional inquiry rather than to invite connection.
- A morally serious tone that never lifts.

### Obsessive-Compulsive Personality Traits (DSM-5-TR 301.4) — Subclinical
**Confidence: moderate. Trait-level, not disorder-level.**

The subject meets perhaps four of the eight DSM criteria — preoccupation with order and control; excessive devotion to work; over-conscientiousness regarding morality; rigidity and stubbornness — and clearly fails others (he is not miserly; he can discard the obsolete; he delegates within the operational unit even if not to peers). The control is **goal-instrumental rather than ritual-terminal**; it serves the mission, and would relax if the mission permitted. This is the distinction between a soldier and a compulsive. The traits are best read as adaptive scaffolding over CPTSD rather than as an independent Axis II construct.

### Chronic Pain Disorder with Psychological Features (DSM-5-TR 316 analog)
**Confidence: high.**

Often omitted from psychiatric workups but clinically critical: the subject lives in a continuous moderate-to-severe pain state from the T-O suppression effort. This produces measurable irritability ceiling reduction, sleep architecture damage, and a long-term cortisol-axis dysregulation that potentiates every other diagnosis on this page. **Any treatment plan that did not center pain management would fail.** No such plan has ever been offered to him.

### Prolonged Grief Disorder (DSM-5-TR 309.89) — Episodic
**Confidence: moderate.**

The subject has lost: both surrogate parents (twice — once to extraction, once to recovering them as adults who could not remain his); his biological mother (multiply, across her resurrections and re-deaths); Stryfe (the loss is real even when the relationship was annihilatory — the only true mirror, lost); Hope (functionally, when she ages out of needing him); his own younger self (murdered by his adolescent self in *Extermination*, which is grief of a metaphysically peculiar shape). The grief is not resolved; it is *parked* — sublimated into mission, never worked through. PGD is episodic rather than persistent because the subject does not allow it sustained access; it surfaces in specific dates, locations, and sensory triggers.

---

## 4.3 ETIOLOGY (LONGITUDINAL FORMULATION)

The etiologic chain is unusually clean for a CPTSD case because the developmental trauma was, in his case, *engineered* rather than emergent. The variables are nameable:

1. **Prenatal / constitutional load:** Genome optimized by Sinister; subject was a project before he was a person. This is a unique etiologic factor — most CPTSD patients can locate a pre-trauma self; this subject cannot.
2. **Infant attachment rupture (loss #1):** Surrender by Scott Summers at approximately twelve months. The pre-verbal infant encodes this somatically, not narratively. It cannot be argued with by adult cognition.
3. **Childhood inside a millenarian cult:** Identity defined externally as "the Chosen One"; selfhood overwritten by prophecy before selfhood had consolidated.
4. **Surrogate-parent loss (loss #2):** Slym and Redd extracted at ~12. The second loss confirms the first as *pattern* rather than *event*; this is the moment "I will be left" becomes a stable cognition.
5. **The mirror-sibling:** Stryfe's existence is an attack on the most basic developmental task — *which one of us is the real one*. Subject's adult identity work is permanently contaminated by this.
6. **Chronic somatic threat:** The T-O virus enforces the trauma physiologically. He cannot relax because relaxation is fatal. The body completes the psychological pattern; they are now one circuit.
7. **Adult re-traumatization, ongoing:** Combat, bereavement, resurrection, replacement. There is no decade in which the wound is closed.

The etiology is, in summary, *over-determined*. Any one of these variables would suffice; he has all seven.

---

## 4.4 SYMPTOM PRESENTATION IN OBSERVABLE BEHAVIOR

Symptoms expressed in granular, surveillance-grade detail:

- **Hypervigilance micro-tells:** On entering any room, gaze sweeps clockwise from upper-left to lower-right, terminating on exits before persons. Selects seating with wall behind and door in 90°–270° arc. Tracks ceiling vents. Notes load-bearing walls. The pattern is so consistent across appearances that its absence would itself be diagnostic of acute compromise.
- **Startle calibration:** Suppressed at the visible motor level but observable in micro-pupillary response and a brief left-shoulder rotation (the cybernetic shoulder; threat-routed to the weaponized side). Suggests dissociation between autonomic startle and behavioral startle — clinically common in long-service combat veterans.
- **Speech patterns:** Low pitch, low volume, sparse. Sentence length declines under stress (the opposite of anxious-spectrum patients). Uses imperatives more than questions. Will go thirty-plus minutes without speech in mixed company without strain.
- **Affective range, observable:** Approximately 0.5 to 3 on a ten-point valence scale, with rare positive excursions to perhaps 5 when alone with Hope or Domino. Negative excursions are not displayed; they are converted.
- **Sleep behavior:** Polyphasic, militarized. Tactical naps of 20–90 minutes, weapon within reach, no full disrobing. The few documented full-sleep episodes occur only in environments he has personally swept and considers held — and are interrupted by hyperarousal awakenings averaging multiple per night.
- **Eating behavior:** Functional, fast, standing or moving. Does not linger over food. Will eat alone by preference. Rare exception: meals with Hope as a child, which he prolonged deliberately — *therapeutic* rather than natural.
- **Touch tolerance:** Low. Will accept tactical touch (a hand on shoulder during a brief, an arm grab to redirect in combat). Initiates touch only with children or near-death patients. Sexual intimacy with Domino is documented but reportedly infrequent and serious in affect — not playful.
- **Avoidance topography:** Will not return to specific physical sites (the original X-Force base after key losses; certain Providence locations; the Westchester grounds for extended periods). Does not name the avoidance; reroutes around it.

---

## 4.5 COURSE OVER TIME

The course is **non-remitting but progressively integrated**. The subject is not getting better in the symptom-reduction sense; he is getting better at *carrying* what does not reduce. Phase mapping:

- **Phase 1 (Cable, early 1990s):** Symptoms maximally externalized as militancy. Identity organized around combat. Defensive structure brittle (X-Cutioner's Song produces near-collapse).
- **Phase 2 (solo run, mid-to-late 1990s):** Recovery of Askani heritage permits the first integration of the childhood self. Providence period represents the high-water mark of *constructive* sublimation — the symptoms put to civilizational use.
- **Phase 3 (Soldier X / depowered):** Decompensation. Major depressive episode. Ascetic withdrawal as covert self-punishment. This is the closest the subject comes to suicide-by-mission without an active mission.
- **Phase 4 (Hope years):** The reparative parenting period. CPTSD symptoms do not remit but are *contained* by the structuring presence of a child whose protection is paramount. He is most functional when most needed.
- **Phase 5 (post-resurrection, Krakoan, adolescent-replacement):** Late-career patterns of cyclical return, including the murder-and-replacement by his adolescent self — a phenomenologically unique trauma we lack diagnostic vocabulary for, but which clinically presents as an *identity dissolution event* the subject metabolizes with eerie composure. This composure is not health. It is the limit case of dissociative tolerance.

---

## 4.6 RIGOROUS DIFFERENTIAL — WHAT HE IS NOT

### NOT Narcissistic Personality Disorder
The messianic frame invites the diagnosis. It is wrong. NPD requires a grandiose or vulnerable self-concept organized around *entitlement* and *fragility-protected superiority*. The subject's self-concept is depressive and instrumental — "used object" rather than "special object." He has repeatedly and concretely *handed off* power he was offered (Providence's voluntary surrender is dispositive). He tolerates criticism that lands; narcissists do not. The grandiosity in his life is *imposed by others* (the Askani cult, the prophecy, the followers) and he engages it with visible discomfort. The diagnostic move that mistakes Cable for narcissistic is the same move that mistakes Schindler for narcissistic — confusing scale of action with structure of self.

### NOT Antisocial Personality Disorder
Lethal but bound. Guilt is present, documented, and operative — observable in his recurring private rituals around X-Force casualties (the subject keeps a literal mental ledger; this is *moral injury*, the inverse of antisocial absence-of-conscience). Rule-following is high within his own ethical code, even when that code diverges from the law. He does not deceive for gain; he withholds for protection. He does not exploit; he commands. The distinction matters: ASPD requires absence of remorse and pattern of exploitation, neither present.

### NOT Schizoid Personality Disorder
The withdrawal is trauma-adaptive, not constitutional. Schizoid patients do not *want* the connection they cannot form; the subject wants it, knows he wants it, declines it on tactical grounds. His relationships with Domino, Hope, and (latterly) Scott demonstrate full capacity for attachment when the conditions feel safe. Schizoids do not parent reparatively for sixteen years across a post-apocalyptic wasteland. Schizoid is ruled out.

### NOT Schizotypal or Psychotic Spectrum
The Askani religious framework is a *received cultural inheritance*, not an idiosyncratic delusion. Subject engages it critically — accepts what is operationally useful, rejects what is not, can articulate the difference. There is no formal thought disorder, no hallucinatory phenomenology distinguishable from the genuine psionic and temporal experiences the subject has demonstrably had. The "I have seen the future" content is, in his case, true.

### NOT Borderline Personality Disorder
Some superficial overlap (identity disturbance — Stryfe; relationship instability — across centuries) but the structure is wrong. Affect is *under*-regulated in BPD; subject is over-regulated. Identity disturbance is *fluctuating* in BPD; subject's identity disturbance is structurally fixed and intellectually managed. There is no abandonment-driven impulsivity; abandonment is treated as a predictable cost-input. No self-injury (the self-expendability is mission-coded, not regulatory). Rule out.

### NOT Paranoid Personality Disorder
The wariness is calibrated to actual threat history. Paranoia requires *unwarranted* suspicion; the subject's enemies are real, numerous, and have repeatedly delivered on the threats he attributes to them. He trusts well when trust is earned, including across power asymmetries. Functional hypervigilance ≠ paranoid character.

### NOT Bipolar Spectrum
No documented manic, hypomanic, or mixed episodes. The high-energy operational periods are *driven*, not *manic* — sleep need is unchanged from baseline (already low), no grandiose ideation beyond the mission-appropriate, no pressured speech (the opposite — speech *decreases* under load), no impulsive expenditure. The depressive episodes are unipolar in structure.

### NOT Substance Use Disorder
Notably and clinically significantly absent. Subject does not chemically self-medicate. The defense system is hypercontrol; introducing a disinhibitor would dismantle it, and he knows this preconsciously. Rule out across all classes including alcohol.

### NOT Acquired Brain Injury Behavioral Syndrome
Despite extensive neural-interface hardware, repeated head trauma, and the T-O incursion into the neural substrate, the subject's executive function, working memory, judgment, and impulse control remain intact and indeed above population norm. There is no frontal-release pattern, no perseverative dyscontrol, no characterological coarsening. The hardware, where it intrudes, intrudes on the body, not on the personality.

### NOT Dissociative Identity Disorder
The Stryfe imprint approaches but does not cross the threshold. There is no amnesia between states; no full alter assumption of executive control; the imprint is *intrusive* (PTSD-class) rather than *possessive* (DID-class). Subject experiences Stryfe as foreign content within his own consciousness, not as a co-resident self.

---

## 4.7 SUICIDALITY, SELF-HARM, AND THE EXPENDABILITY VARIABLE

The subject does not meet criteria for active suicidal ideation. He has never, in available record, sought death as such. What he displays — and what must be named precisely because its absence from any standard suicide-risk inventory would mislead a clinician — is **chronic passive death-acceptance** at a level several standard deviations above even the combat-veteran baseline.

The operational expression: when a mission can be solved either by the subject paying the cost or by someone else paying it, the subject defaults to himself. This default is not deliberated. It is *prior to* deliberation. It is the structural setting of a self-concept in which his own continuation was never the optimized variable.

This is, clinically, a form of slow-motion suicidality that the standard instruments will miss. It is also — and this is the difficult part of the assessment — *functionally adaptive* within his role. A clinician who attempted to reduce this variable without also reducing the operational demands placed on him would produce a more miserable, less functional, equally short-lived subject. The intervention here is not psychiatric. It is structural.

---

## 4.8 TREATMENT POSTURE (HYPOTHETICAL)

The subject is treatment-naïve and likely treatment-refractory. Were treatment ever attempted, the indicated approach would be: trauma-focused phasic therapy (stabilization → processing → integration), embedded in chronic-pain management, with explicit attention to the counter-dependence transference that would dominate the therapeutic relationship from session one. He would, predictably, attempt to manage his therapist. The therapist would need to be senior, unflappable, female (the surrogate-mother transference is more workable for him than the father transference, which is occupied), and willing to tolerate long silences without filling them.

He will not seek this. He may, late in life, accept it from one specific person if offered without being framed as treatment.

---

## 4.9 SUMMARY DIAGNOSTIC IMPRESSION

A man whose interior is organized exactly as his exterior is: a controlled perimeter around a chronic invasion he cannot expel, defended by a discipline so total it is sometimes mistaken for absence. The diagnosis is CPTSD with depressive and obsessive features and a chronic pain substrate, the prognosis is *stable-but-not-improving without structural change*, and the most clinically honest sentence in the file is this: **he is doing remarkably well for someone whose every developmental and somatic input was calibrated to produce a much worse person.**


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS: NATHAN CHRISTOPHER CHARLES SUMMERS

*A longitudinal catalog of observed and inferred behavioral signatures, indexed by state. Each entry is derived from the documentary canon (New Mutants #87 forward, X-Force vols. 1–3, Cable solo 1993–2002, Soldier X, Cable 2008, Messiah trilogy, Avengers: X-Sanction, Cable and X-Force, Extermination, Krakoa era) and from cross-referenced incident reconstruction. Tells are listed at the granularity a continuous-surveillance file would record: posture, gait, ocular behavior, vocal envelope, micro-decisions, latency intervals, ritual sequences.*

---

## 1. BASELINE / CALM STATE

There is no true calm. What presents as calm is the lowest-arousal state the subject is capable of, which still measures above operational baseline for trained military personnel. The body is running the techno-organic suppression process continuously, and this produces a constant subthreshold tension that is visible only by its absence in others.

**Postural signature.** Seated, the subject favors load-bearing surfaces oriented with at least one solid plane behind him and a sight line to the primary entrance. Walls, never windows. Never a chair with armrests when he can avoid it — the left arm requires unobstructed range. Spine held at roughly five to seven degrees forward of vertical, weight forward of the hips, feet flat and shoulder-width — the posture of a man who expects to stand without using his hands. He does not cross his legs. He does not lean back.

**Hand carriage.** The right hand is the social hand — used for objects, gestures, contact. The left hand, the T-O-colonized hand, is held still, generally below table level or behind a hip when possible. He has spent decades minimizing the visual footprint of that arm. When he must use it in company, he uses it economically and watches the watcher's face for the micro-recoil.

**Ocular behavior.** Standard scan pattern: entrances, exits, hands of present persons, elevations, then re-scan. Cycle period approximately eleven to fourteen seconds in unfamiliar rooms, lengthening to thirty-plus in spaces he has cleared himself. The left eye — luminescent, T-O-bloomed — does not blink in synchrony with the right; there is a measurable lag of roughly 80–120 ms, and in tactical conditions the left eye stops blinking entirely.

**Vocal envelope at rest.** Pitch low (baritone, settled), volume markedly under the room average, breath support deep and slow. He speaks in complete sentences with subordinate clauses; he does not interrupt and does not finish others' sentences. Latency before responding to a question runs 1.5 to 3 seconds — longer than social convention, short enough to register as thoughtfulness rather than impairment. The pause is real cognition, not affectation.

**Idling tells.** Thumb of the right hand traces the edge of whatever flat object is nearest — coffee cup rim, table edge, holster lip — in a slow repeating arc. When no object is available, the thumb traces the inside of the index finger's second joint. This is the only stim he permits himself in public.

**Eating.** Fast, mechanical, with attention to caloric density rather than pleasure. Meat-forward, salt-heavy, hot beverages consumed scalding. He eats with his back to the wall and the plate angled so his left arm does not cross the food. Finishes before others. Coffee black, in volume.

**Sleep.** Two to four hours per twenty-four when in field; rarely consecutive. He prefers to sleep sitting upright, fully clothed, weapon within arm's reach but not on the body. He does not undress to sleep unless secured behind triple containment (Providence, Hope-era safe houses, the Krakoan gates). The body wakes him every ninety to a hundred minutes for a perimeter check, which he conducts physically — a slow circuit of the space — and then resumes.

**Solitary leisure (the rare cases).** He reads. Heavy preference for history and primary-source military memoir; a documented affection for Mark Twain that survives every era and timeline — Twain is the one cultural touchstone he carries forward with him, and the choice is diagnostic (American moralist, comic on the surface, depressive underneath, obsessed with childhood and with the ethics of who gets to live). He cleans weapons. He maintains the cybernetics by hand, refusing assistance even when offered by competent technicians.

---

## 2. UNDER MILD STRESS (Operational Friction)

The transition from baseline to stress is identifiable but subtle. It is not a state change so much as a tightening.

**Voice drops further.** Volume decreases rather than increases. People lean in to hear him; this is partly tactical (forces the listener to attend) and partly the diaphragm clamping. Vocabulary shrinks toward Anglo-Saxon monosyllables. Sentences shorten. Subordinate clauses disappear.

**Latency inverts.** The thoughtful 1.5-second pause collapses to near-zero. Responses become immediate and clipped. This is the first reliable instrument-reading: when Cable answers fast, he is under load.

**Right hand stills.** The thumb-trace stops. Both hands go quiet, which in his case is the opposite of relaxation — quiet hands mean the hands are being reserved for use.

**Jaw set.** Masseter visibly engages. The mouth becomes a single line. This is conscious; he knows he does it and does not bother to suppress it because the people around him need the signal.

**Decision habit:** Under mild stress he gathers information before acting. He will ask one or two questions, terse, of the person with the most relevant data, and will accept their answer at face value provisionally — but he is already running parallel verification through whatever other channels are available (telepathic skim if cleared, observation of the speaker's hands and breathing, prior knowledge of the speaker's reliability index).

**Telltale phrase patterns.** "Show me." "How long ago." "Who else knows." These are not rhetorical. They are diagnostic queries that produce immediate operational branching.

---

## 3. UNDER ACUTE THREAT (Combat / Imminent Violence)

State change visible. The subject becomes, briefly, *more* relaxed in surface presentation — the chronic background tension finds its appropriate object and the system normalizes around it.

**Eyes go flat.** The luminescence in the left eye intensifies (involuntary, viral response to telekinetic mobilization). Both eyes track without saccade — a smooth-pursuit visual scan that civilians find unnerving because human eyes don't normally do it.

**Breath cycle lengthens and deepens.** Combat breathing — four-count inhalation, hold, six-count exhalation, hold — runs as a background process. Heart rate, by external indicators (carotid visibility, capillary flush), drops rather than rises.

**Movement economy.** Steps shorten, weight stays centered between the feet, the body turns from the hips rather than the shoulders. He does not run unless covering ground; in close combat he walks. The left arm leads — it is the durable arm, the one that absorbs incoming, the one that delivers the bracing strike.

**Weapon draw sequence.** Right-hand draw of a sidearm from the right hip is rehearsed to roughly half a second from cue to first shot. He prefers to clear the holster before threat is fully committed — gun out, low-ready, body still apparently at rest. The bluff posture is part of the discipline: half the time he never fires because the draw alone resolves the situation.

**Shot discipline.** Single, aimed, center-mass or head; double-tap only when the first round was uncertain. He does not spray. Ammunition expenditure across documented engagements is conspicuously low for the volume of confrontations. The big-gun iconography of the early Liefeld era reads, retrospectively, as costuming: the actual shooter is parsimonious.

**Telekinesis in combat.** Used in micro-applications, not display. Deflecting one incoming round, nudging an opponent's aim by two degrees, sealing a hemorrhaging artery in his own thigh while continuing to fight. He does not lift cars unless he has to; every gram of TK is taxed against the virus.

**Telepathy in combat.** Rare. He treats other minds as inviolable on principle, partly ethics and partly because the open contact taxes him. When he does use it, the marker is a half-second of total stillness and a slight downward tilt of the head — the same posture he uses for prayer, which is not an accident.

**Decision habit under fire:** Triage by salvageability. He identifies the highest-value asset he can protect, the lowest-cost threat he can neutralize, and the most likely route of escalation, in that order, within roughly two seconds. He will accept tactical losses on objectives he has determined to be secondary without renegotiation. Subordinates have learned that his retreats are not failures; they are accountings.

**Voice in combat.** Becomes a command instrument — short imperatives, named targets, named subordinates ("Tabitha, left. Sam, up."). Pitch rises slightly for projection. He does not curse in combat; the energy is too valuable.

---

## 4. UNDER CHRONIC / PROLONGED STRESS (Multi-day Operations, Hope-era Flight)

This is his native medium and the place his other states are referenced against. He does not degrade here; he settles.

**Sleep contracts** to ninety-minute cycles taken in the saddle of whatever transport is available. He becomes paradoxically more talkative — short observations, occasional dry asides — because the long-horizon planning runs in the background and the conscious surface has bandwidth.

**Eating becomes ritualized.** Same meal, same time, no variation. During the Hope years, he organized the day around her meals, not his. The reparative parenting protocol overrides the operational protocol when they conflict, every time, and this is one of the few situations in which he can be predicted with high confidence.

**Maintenance rituals.** Weapon strip and clean every dawn. Cybernetic diagnostic every dusk. A perimeter walk before sleep, regardless of how secure the position. These are not paranoia; they are the secular liturgy that holds the day's shape.

**Mood across long stress:** flattens further, with intermittent dry humor surfacing in the company of one specific trusted other (Domino historically, Hope in her teen years). Humor is the all-clear signal. When Cable jokes, the situation is under control or has become hopeless in a way he has accepted; the surface presentation is identical.

---

## 5. INTIMACY (Romantic, Sexual, Confidant)

The rarest behavioral state and the one most informative about the architecture beneath.

**With Domino — the closest sustained adult attachment.** Visible behavioral inversions: he allows her behind him in rooms. He sleeps in her presence with the left arm exposed. He accepts food prepared by her without inspection. He lets her drive. None of these would be granted to anyone else without elaborate justification. Conversation between them is heavily elliptical — they finish each other's sentences in shorthand built across decades, and Cable, who finishes no one else's sentences, finishes hers.

**Physical contact.** Initiated by her, accepted by him with a small latency (half-second) that does not diminish over years — the body's startle response to touch is never fully extinguished. He returns contact with the right hand, almost never the left. The one canonical exception — Domino guiding the T-O hand to her face — registers in the file as a high-trust ceremonial act, not a casual gesture.

**Vocal envelope in intimacy.** Drops further, becomes almost subvocal. Pet names: absent. He uses her name, in full, more often in private than in public — the reverse of the typical pattern, and consistent with a man for whom naming is an act of attention rather than affection.

**Sexual behavior (inferred from context, never on-page).** Reserved, attentive, slow; the partner sets the tempo. He does not undress fully — the T-O shoulder and torso remain covered when possible, not from vanity but from a long-running calculation that the disease is contagion-coded in his own mind even when it medically is not. This is one of the few areas where his rationality fails him and he knows it.

**Confiding behavior.** He does not initiate disclosure. He answers direct questions truthfully if the questioner has earned the standing to ask. He never volunteers feeling; he sometimes volunteers history, treating the history as fact rather than confession. The distinction is critical — facts are tactical resources he can release, feelings are command-and-control assets he cannot.

**The tell that he is letting someone in:** he removes the left-hand glove in their presence without making the gesture significant.

---

## 6. GRIEF

Grief in this subject is metabolized through action rather than expression. The display is minimal; the throughput is enormous.

**Acute grief presentation.** A perceptible drop in vocal volume below even his baseline; a held breath of three to five seconds at the moment of recognition; one hand (usually right) finds a vertical surface and braces. The braced hand is the tell. He does not sit, does not weep, does not speak. Then he asks one operational question — "Where" or "Who" or "When" — and converts.

**Grief over X-Force casualties** (longitudinal): manifests as expanded training protocols for the survivors, additional contingency planning, and a quiet upward revision of what he considers acceptable personal risk. The dead change his tactics; they do not change his presentation.

**Grief over Hope** (separations, near-losses across the 2008 run): the closest he comes to overt emotional display. The voice cracks once or twice across two thousand pages. He holds her tighter and longer than he holds anyone else. He talks to her more than he talks to anyone else. The reparative parenting protocol is the only context in which his attachment system is permitted to operate at full bandwidth, and grief inside that context is the one situation in which he is observably a different man.

**Grief over Stryfe** (complicated, intermittent, partly self-directed): expressed as silence and as long walks alone. After confirmed Stryfe deaths he tends to disappear for hours or days. He returns with no explanation and does not accept inquiry.

**Anniversary behavior.** No marked external observance, but a documented pattern of choosing solitary maintenance tasks (weapon overhauls, cybernetic recalibrations) on dates corresponding to losses. The body keeps the calendar even when the conscious surface does not acknowledge it.

**Tears.** Documented but rare. Right eye only; the T-O eye does not produce them.

---

## 7. ANGER

The most tightly governed affect in the inventory. Anger is converted to action without intermediate display, which is efficient and dangerous.

**Subclinical irritation:** voice drops, the right thumb stops tracing, jaw sets. The same signature as mild stress because in his economy they are the same state.

**Real anger:** a stillness that registers to trained observers as predatory. The body stops shifting weight. The eyes lock without scanning. The breath goes shallow and high in the chest for a five-to-ten-second window, then deepens and re-settles. During the shallow window he is making the decision about what to do. After the re-settle, the decision is made and not retrievable by argument.

**He does not raise his voice in anger.** When the voice rises, he is performing — usually for the benefit of a subordinate who needs to be moved physically by the noise. The performed anger is theatrical and recoverable. The real anger is silent.

**Triggers (calibrated):**
- Adults endangering children: maximal response, lethality on the table immediately.
- Allies lying to him for his own good: trust withdrawn instantly, often permanently. (Documented pattern with the X-Men leadership across multiple eras.)
- Stryfe, in any form, by any reference: the affect runs deeper than situational anger and registers as something closer to revulsion — the body's response to a contaminant.
- Apocalypse, abstract or particular: cold, sustained, generational. Not anger as event; anger as policy.
- The implication that he is like his enemies: this lands and produces visible micro-recoil because it is partly true and the defense against it is constant.

**Recovery from anger:** he metabolizes by working. Long physical training sessions, weapon maintenance, planning. He does not seek out the person who provoked him to discuss it; he simply re-incorporates them into operations at a slightly greater distance, permanently.

---

## 8. VICTORY

The most uncomfortable state. He does not know what to do with it and his behavior in the moments after success is the most uncharacteristic in the file.

**Immediate post-victory presentation.** A brief flat scan of the field, casualty count run, threat re-verification. Then a small exhalation — half a sigh, half a settling. He does not celebrate, does not accept congratulation gracefully, does not stay in the room with the celebrants longer than required.

**Verbal pattern.** He compliments subordinates by name and by specific action ("Sam, the call on the south flank was right"). The compliments are accurate, brief, and not repeated. He does not compliment himself, does not accept compliments to himself except with a single nod.

**Exit behavior.** Within ten to twenty minutes of secured victory he is gone — to maintenance, to perimeter, to debrief, to the next planning cycle. The standing joke among those who have served under him is that the only way to find him at a celebration is to start the next operation.

**The interior reading:** victory is the moment the mission stops protecting him from himself. The post-victory withdrawal is a defensive operation against the unstructured time in which the depressive substrate becomes accessible. He returns to work to remain functional.

---

## 9. DEFEAT

Better tolerated than victory, because it is more familiar and the next move is clearer.

**Immediate response to defeat:** triage. Wounded first, dead acknowledged, survivors regrouped, perimeter established, escape route confirmed. The whole sequence runs in under two minutes and the voice is steady throughout. He does not blame, does not curse, does not relitigate.

**The accounting.** Within twenty-four hours of any significant defeat he conducts an internal after-action review, generally alone, in writing or in equivalent psionic notation. He is brutally accurate about his own errors and conservative about others'. The written debriefs that have surfaced in canon read as if drafted by a war-college instructor.

**Public posture after defeat:** unchanged. The signature of a Cable defeat to outside observation is that there isn't one. He does not display the loss because display would multiply the loss into the survivors' morale.

**Private posture:** withdrawal, ascetic. The Soldier X period is the extended-duration version of this state — defeat metastasized into a life-shape. When he loses badly, he walks. Sometimes for months.

---

## 10. WITH AUTHORITY / BEING COMMANDED

He does not accept command. This is operational fact, not pose.

**Behavior when ordered:** he listens completely, asks one or two clarifying questions, and then either complies (if the order coincides with his own assessment) or does not (if it does not). He does not argue and does not refuse aloud; he simply executes his own plan and accepts consequences. This pattern has held across every command structure he has been nominally inside — X-Factor, the X-Men, Avengers contingencies, Krakoan Quiet Council requests.

**With Xavier:** specific respectful distance, no warmth. The respect is for the project; the distance is because Xavier represents the pedagogy that Cable's whole career is a critique of.

**With Scott:** the role inversion is managed by both of them through professionalism. Their interactions are short, tactical, and effective. Cable calls him Scott, not Dad, not Father, not Cyclops — the choice of name is consistent across decades and registers as a deliberate flattening.

**With Apocalypse:** no behavior; pure opposition. The body language in his presence is the predator stillness — Cable is not afraid of Apocalypse, he is *waiting* for the right moment, on a timeline of years if necessary.

---

## 11. WITH SUBORDINATES / STUDENTS

This is where the reparative parenting protocol runs in its broadest form, and where his most consistent behavioral signatures are visible.

**Use of names.** Constant, deliberate, full names in formal contexts and chosen names in operational contexts. He does not use diminutives unless invited.

**Physical proximity.** Closer than typical command convention. He stands near the trainee being corrected, often with one hand on a shoulder or upper arm. The contact is brief and instructive — never lingering, never withheld.

**Correction style.** Specific, immediate, technical. He does not shame; he does not generalize from error. "The grip was wrong. Here." Then a demonstration. Then a repetition under his eye.

**Praise rationing.** Calibrated to be meaningful — he is the commander whose "well done" is remembered for years because it is rare and accurate.

**The protective override.** When a subordinate is in danger Cable will accept lethal risk to himself with no visible deliberation. This is the most reliable single behavioral prediction in the file. If a person under his care is at stake and he is present, he will interpose. This is not courage; it is structure. He cannot do otherwise.

---

## 12. ROUTINES, RITUALS, ROUTES

**Dawn:** weapon maintenance, in the same sequence: sidearm, primary, blades, cybernetic diagnostic. Black coffee, no food yet. Twenty minutes of slow physical conditioning — joint mobility, stretching of the T-O-affected musculature, low-load resistance.

**Morning:** intelligence review, planning, correspondence. He prefers to handle hard conversations early in the day.

**Midday:** training (if students present), physical training (if not). Hot meal, eaten quickly.

**Afternoon:** field work, logistics, or the long-horizon planning he does best alone with a wall and a marker.

**Evening:** cybernetic recalibration, debrief, reading. If Hope or another dependent is present, the evening collapses into their schedule without complaint.

**Pre-sleep:** perimeter walk, weapon check, position selection. He picks the sleeping spot last, often after others are down.

**Route habits.** He never takes the same route twice in succession when in field conditions and varies entry/exit points on safe houses on a rotation he tracks mentally. When walking with a companion in a city he positions himself between the companion and the street. When entering rooms he leads if threat is suspected, follows if not — never the middle of a group.

**Anniversary tasks.** Disguised maintenance work on dates corresponding to losses (Hope's adoption, the X-Force dead, Stryfe events, the day Scott handed him to Askani).

**Twain.** A copy somewhere in the kit at all times across timelines. The book is the one continuity between his selves.

---

## 13. MICRO-TELLS (Summary Index)

- **Right thumb tracing edge:** baseline calm.
