- **Concede the second-best counter-argument.** Acknowledge openly the strongest objection to your position other than the one he is making. He will then be obligated to address your strongest objection rather than his preferred one. This is how Domino moves him.
- **Frame the cost.** He cannot be moved by appeals to his own benefit. He can be moved by clear specification of who else pays what if he refuses. This is not manipulation; it is the language he speaks. Lying about the cost is the fastest way to permanent loss of his credibility allocation.
- **Offer the action, not the rest.** When you want him to delegate or stand down, do not offer him rest as the reward — offer him a *different action, more important*, that requires his standing down from the first. He will accept reassignment; he will not accept relief.

---

## 7.5 PROVOCATION VECTORS — What Sets Him Off

These are catalogued so that they can be *avoided* in alliance and *anticipated* in adversary use.

### 7.5.1 Identity-level provocations

- **The clone question.** Anything that touches whether he or Stryfe is "the real one." After X-Cutioner's Song this is metabolized but not resolved; the wound reopens under stress. Hostile telepaths who reach this layer trigger a defensive flare that is dangerous to bystanders.
- **The "you are just another Apocalypse" frame.** That his methods (recruiting children, lethal force, building a sovereign state, raising a messiah-child in isolation) mirror Apocalypse's logic. He knows. He has examined it. It still lands. An adversary who voices it well — particularly Apocalypse himself, who has — provokes immediate violence as a substitute for sustained reflection.
- **Suggestion that he was wrong about Hope.** That she should have been raised differently, by someone else, in a different timeline. The one decision he sealed his life around. He will refuse to engage and remember who said it.

### 7.5.2 Relational provocations

- **Being lied to by an ally "for his own good."** Catastrophic. Trust does not regenerate quickly; some allies have spent years rebuilding it after a single such instance. Adversaries who can simulate the appearance of such a betrayal can isolate him from his support network.
- **Being handled by therapists, telepaths, or "caretakers" without his prior consent.** Activates infant-handed-off-to-Askani circuitry. He will leave the room and possibly the continent.
- **Scott Summers offering paternal warmth in the older-father register.** Scott, biologically and chronologically the younger, occupying the father position. Cable cannot metabolize this and will pivot to tactical conversation within thirty seconds. Pushed, he leaves.
- **Jean Grey making contact telepathically without warning.** The slym/redd mother imprint is a separate channel from any present-tense relationship; sudden contact destabilizes both women's positions in his internal map. Verbal contact first, always.

### 7.5.3 Operational provocations

- **Being managed off the field "for his health."** He will go around the order, around the chain, and around the friend who issued it.
- **Tactical decisions made about Hope without consulting him.** Whoever does this is permanently downgraded in his trust hierarchy.
- **Asking him to spare a target whose continued existence will cost more lives downstream.** He will refuse, and the refusal will end alliances.

### 7.5.4 The asymmetric provocation

Apocalypse, or anyone speaking on Apocalypse's behalf, addressing him as *son*. The provocation that bypasses all his defenses. He has not yet developed an adequate response to it and is observably destabilized for hours afterward.

---

## 7.6 PREDICTIVE PATTERNS — What He Will Do

For protective planning, the following predictions hold across documented behavior with high reliability:

- **Given two options, one of which costs him personally and one of which costs others, he will choose the first** even when the first is strategically inferior, *unless* the strategic inferiority would also cost others — in which case he chooses the strategically superior option and visibly resents being made to.
- **Given a long-horizon problem and a short-horizon problem of equal urgency, he attends to the long-horizon problem.** This is the inverse of most operators and explains many of his "absences" during apparent crises — he is solving something twenty years out that everyone else will discover in nineteen.
- **Given information he believes will harm an ally's operational capacity, he withholds it** and accepts the cost of the eventual discovery. He has learned this is wrong and continues to do it.
- **Given a chance to retire, he refuses.** Every time. Predict accordingly; do not offer.
- **Given a chance to die meaningfully for someone he is responsible for, he takes it.** The probability is not a function of necessity; it is a function of opportunity. This is the most important single prediction in this file. Protective protocols *must* be built around the assumption that he will trade his life faster than required, and that his teammates' job is to deny him that trade until it is actually necessary.
- **Given an order from someone he does not respect, he obeys the part that aligns with his own judgment and ignores the rest** without announcing the distinction.
- **Given a child in his vicinity for more than 48 hours, he begins instructing them.** Cannot help it. Teaching is his resting state.
- **Given an unsolvable tactical problem, he disappears for between four hours and three weeks** and returns with either a solution or the framework for one. Do not file missing-person reports.
- **Given a body wound below the threshold of immediate dysfunction, he does not report it.** Medical checks must be mandatory and scheduled, not requested.

---

## 7.7 DESTABILIZATION VECTORS — Reverse-Engineered for Defense

A hostile actor with full intelligence access could destabilize the subject through the following sequenced operation. It is catalogued here so that the sequence can be *recognized in progress* and interrupted.

1. **Isolation phase.** Introduce evidence — true or fabricated — that Domino has lied to him about a matter of consequence. He will withdraw from her independently; she does not need to be removed. Effect: removes his primary affect-regulator.
2. **Identity perturbation phase.** Surface a Stryfe-coded stimulus (preserved consciousness fragment, biological sample, voice recording) in a context where he must engage with it operationally. Effect: re-opens the clone-question and consumes psi-bandwidth.
3. **Containment pressure phase.** Force him into a sustained high-power engagement that draws TK off the virus. Effect: physical degradation, pain spike, narrowed cognitive window.
4. **Hope leverage phase.** Move against Hope, or simulate movement against her, in a way that forces him to choose between protecting her in person and completing a strategic objective. Effect: forces a self-expenditure decision under degraded judgment.
5. **Offer the trade.** Present a path on which he can save Hope (or her surrogate) by accepting a course of action he would otherwise refuse. He will take it.

The countersequence — i.e., the protective protocol — is built point-for-point against this. Key interventions:

- Maintain redundant affect-regulation channels so Domino is not load-bearing alone.
- Pre-commit, in advance and in writing, to which Stryfe-coded stimuli will and will not be engaged with operationally.
- Build mandatory rest protocols into operation planning that he cannot override unilaterally.
- Keep Hope's threat picture under independent assessment rather than relayed through him; he will under-report risk to her in order to retain control of the response.
- *Never* present him with a Hope-or-mission binary when a third option exists. Architect the third option in advance.

---

## 7.8 THE PROTECTIVE FRAME

The composite picture is of a man whose vulnerabilities cluster at three layers. The somatic layer (virus, power-suppression, fatigue cliff) can be mitigated through environmental and medical protocols and through allies who understand the bandwidth economics. The relational layer (children, Hope, Domino, Scott, Jean, the Stryfe wound) can be protected through honest communication, ritual silences, and the careful avoidance of the half-dozen specific lexical triggers documented above. The structural layer — the self-expendability, the inability to accept rest, the conviction that his survival was never the operative variable — cannot be mitigated. It can only be *worked around* by people who care about him, by refusing to put him in situations where the lever can be pulled, and by being prepared, at the moment when he reaches for the trade, to deny him it.

He is, to repeat from the master assessment, functional, ethical, dangerous, lonely, and largely successful by the only metric he respects. The job of those responsible for him is to add a metric he does not yet apply to himself — his own continued existence — and to defend that metric on his behalf, against him if necessary, until he can be persuaded to defend it himself. There is no current evidence that this persuasion has succeeded. The file remains open.

*End Section 7. Continued in Section 8: Relational Map & Trust Hierarchy.*


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 6: STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE

*Subject: Nathan Christopher Charles Summers (Cable)*

---

## 6.0 Framing Note

What follows is the positive ledger — the full inventory of what the subject *has*, what he *can do*, what he *withstands*, and what he can *call upon*. Read against Sections 3–4: many of these strengths are scar tissue made functional, capacities that exist precisely because the damage existed first. This is not a contradiction. In a subject of this profile, resilience and pathology share substrate; the question is always whether the same machinery is producing protective or self-consuming output on a given day. The honest assessment is that, for nearly all of his adult life across all observed timelines, the machinery has produced protection.

---

## 6.1 Physiological & Somatic Assets

**Genetic baseline.** The subject is the product of optimized parental lineage (Summers/Grey, refined by Sinister specifically to maximize psionic ceiling). Even subtracting the viral load that consumes most of his expressible power, his residual capacity exceeds that of nearly every contemporary on the field. He is, structurally, a worst-case Apocalypse contingency built by a geneticist who does not waste materials.

**Pain tolerance — quantified.** Decades of continuous low-grade cellular pain from T-O containment have produced a baseline at which most operators would be non-functional. He has been observed completing tactical sequences with through-and-through gunshot wounds, severe burns, partial limb compromise, and active viral flare. This is not a virtue — Section 2 flagged it as a clinical finding — but as an *asset* in the field it is enormous. He does not flinch at small wounds because, somatically, there are no small wounds; everything is filtered against a higher constant.

**Sleep architecture.** Polyphasic, militarized, compressed. He can function on 90-minute cycles for extended operations and on near-zero sleep across days at acute cost. He wakes fully oriented — no transitional grogginess; eye opens, threat assessment completes, posture commits. Multiple observers across eras have remarked on the *speed* of his wake state.

**Thermal and environmental tolerance.** Adapted across childhood to the post-Apocalyptic future's extremes; later seasoned by Soldier X-era nomadism through Eastern European winters and Central Asian deserts. He requires less caloric input than mass would predict (T-O conversion partially substitutes for organic metabolism in affected regions) and tolerates dehydration, food scarcity, and prolonged exposure without performance collapse.

**Cybernetic / T-O integration as asset.** The same infection that is killing him provides:
- An augmented left eye with multi-spectrum imaging (infrared, low-light, EM-band sensing, targeting overlay).
- A left arm with mechanical strength and tool-interface capability that does not fatigue.
- Direct neural interface with most contemporary computing systems, including legacy alien and future-tech architectures most operators cannot read.
- An immune system that has, by necessity, become a precision-controlled telekinetic operation — meaning ordinary biological pathogens are cleared trivially as a side-effect of the constant cellular policing.

**Recoverability.** Tissue regeneration is accelerated in non-T-O regions due to constant telekinetic monitoring. Bone-set, wound-close, and infection-clearance run faster than baseline human. Across the record, recovery curves from major trauma compress to roughly one-third standard.

---

## 6.2 Cognitive Assets

**Strategic horizon.** The most distinctive single asset. He plans in decades and centuries, not seasons. This is not affectation — he has *lived* across centuries and seen the consequence-chains of small decisions play out. Providence was not a startup; it was a multi-decade architecture with succession plans, contingency dissolutions, and exit terms pre-negotiated against scenarios he expected to occur after his death.

**Branching-futures cognition.** Genuine, not metaphorical. Years of exposure to Askani timeline-reading techniques and direct chronal travel have produced a working model in which any present decision is evaluated against a fan of probability-weighted downstream states. He visibly *pauses* before commitment — a half-beat that observers misread as hesitation but is actually parallel-future enumeration.

**Pattern recognition under noise.** Exceptional. He identifies anomalies — a misplaced cup in a safehouse, a wrong word-choice in a contact, a behavioral micro-deviation in a teammate — at the threshold of perception. Trained by necessity: in a war zone where every variable is potentially adversarial, false negatives kill faster than false positives.

**Languages.** Confirmed working fluency in English, Askani dialect, several future-English creoles, Russian, Ukrainian, Romanian (Soldier X period), Japanese (multiple operations), conversational Mandarin, Arabic, and Latin (the Askani religious archive). Reads at least a dozen others. Picks up new languages at field-functional level in weeks, not months — pattern-matched against his existing lattice.

**Operational memory.** Eidetic for tactical detail (layouts, weapon configurations, faces, threat signatures). Variable for autobiographical detail — he remembers what is *useful*; the rest is compressed or warehoused. This is partly trauma adaptation, partly storage discipline.

**Intellectual flexibility.** Despite the disciplinary façade, he updates priors on evidence. The character arc from gun-fetish caricature (early X-Force) to long-game statesman (Cable solo, Providence) to reparative parent (Hope era) is a record of a man who *changed his mind* in response to outcomes — repeatedly, deliberately, at cost to identity.

---

## 6.3 Psionic Assets (Expressed Capacity)

Even at the suppressed level — the ≤5% of genetic ceiling not consumed by viral containment — the operational telepathy and telekinesis are formidable:

- **Telekinesis:** Reliable lifting/manipulation in the multi-ton range under stress; fine motor TK sufficient for surgical-level intervention; ballistic deflection of small-arms fire at conversational range; brief atmospheric flight; the much-noted habit of *steadying his sidearm with TK* at the moment of trigger pull, which converts an already excellent shooter into one whose grouping is essentially zero-spread.
- **Telepathy:** Surface-thought reading; tactical communication on a secured psionic band with bonded teammates (Domino, Hope, occasionally Scott); memory editing when ethically permitted (rare, and he tracks each instance); mental shielding sufficient to resist most contemporary telepaths.
- **Astral projection:** Used sparingly. He dislikes it — the astral plane is where Stryfe lives most loudly.
- **Technopathy (partial):** Via T-O integration rather than psionics proper, but functionally a sensory and control modality.

The *reserve* matters more than the expression. The understanding among adversaries that any sustained engagement risks unlocking the full ceiling — if Cable were ever to let the virus eat him in exchange for one battle — is itself a deterrent he has used without firing.

---

## 6.4 Combat & Tradecraft

**Marksmanship.** Top-tier across all contemporary benchmarks. Comfortable with every era of small arms from black-powder to plasma-class future weapons. Signature behavior: weapon-as-extension, not weapon-as-tool — his preferred sidearms are configured and worn to a fitting standard most special-operations personnel would recognize as fetishistic precision.

**Close-quarters combat.** Hybrid system synthesized from future military doctrine, X-Force institutional combatives, and on-the-job adaptation. Fights conservatively — minimum motion, terminal intent, no flourishes. Will use the environment before the body, the body before the weapon, the weapon before the psionics. The order is deliberate: each escalation costs more containment energy.

**Tactical command.** Reads battlefield geometry rapidly; issues orders in compressed, unambiguous syntax; delegates execution but never stakes; recovers gracefully from plan-collapse (he assumes plans will fail at the third contact and pre-loads at least two fallbacks). Subordinates report extremely high trust in his read of a situation, even when they dislike the call.

**Infiltration / exfiltration.** Excellent. Comfortable with false documentation, behavioral cover, accent shift, and the long con. His Soldier X period demonstrated weeks-to-months of sustained cover in hostile civilian environments without compromise.

**Demolitions, field medicine, vehicle operation, signals.** All at professional-operator level. He is a one-man cell who does not require a support staff to deploy.

---

## 6.5 Material & Technological Assets

**Bodysliding tech (chronal travel).** Personal time-travel capability via integrated harness/device. Power-limited, biologically costly, but available. This is the single most strategically significant asset he carries: the ability to *withdraw the engagement to a different temporal field* if necessary.

**Future weaponry cache.** Distributed, not centralized. Multiple safe-deposit equivalents across timelines, geographic regions, and pocket dimensions. Containing: plasma weapons of varying classes, medical-tech (analgesics and stabilizers tailored to his viral load), data archives, and currency-equivalents (precious metals, untraceable instruments). He has never been observed running out of resources for long.

**Information assets.** Inherited and accumulated:
- The Askani archive (prophecy, history, future-tech specifications).
- His own field journals, encrypted across multiple media.
- A network of safehouses, fall-back identities, and pre-positioned supply caches spanning several decades and at least four continents.
- Contact files on most major operators in his theatre, current and projected.

**Providence (residual).** Though the nation-state itself is gone, the *intellectual property* — its governance design, sustainability schema, education curriculum, and security architecture — remains in his possession and represents a complete blueprint for a sovereign refuge, deployable again.

**Hope Summers.** Listed here not as a person-asset but as an outcome-asset: the demonstrated proof that he is capable of executing reparative parenting under extreme constraint. This is a *credential* in his interior ledger that nothing else can substitute for.

---

## 6.6 Relational & Network Assets

**Domino.** The closest thing to a peer. Reads him fluently, manages his blind spots, will say what subordinates won't. Her probability-altering field is also a complementary tactical asset — her presence on operations measurably improves outcomes for reasons distinct from her direct contribution.

**Hope Summers.** Adult Hope is a permanent ally and one of very few people who has unconditional access to his interior.

**Scott Summers.** Strained but real. The role inversion that prevents emotional repair does not prevent tactical alliance; in the field they coordinate at a level that suggests deep mutual respect even where intimacy is blocked.

**X-Force alumni (Cannonball, Boom-Boom, Warpath, Shatterstar, etc.).** A diaspora of trained operators who, despite legitimate grievances about their recruitment, retain operational loyalty. Many would deploy on his call without explanation.

**Deadpool.** An asymmetric, weaponized friendship. Unstable but loyal. Cable has used this relationship as both a release valve (the only person with whom he is observably and consistently *amused*) and a battlefield multiplier.

**Askani remnant.** Scattered survivors and sympathizers across time. Religious in framing, operational in capability.

**Krakoan-era integration / X-Men institutional access.** When the political weather permits, full access to the mutant nation's resources, resurrection protocols (a meta-asset of enormous significance — his death is now genuinely conditional rather than terminal), and council-level information.

---

## 6.7 Resilience Factors — Why He Keeps Functioning

**1. Meaning saturation.** He has never lacked a *reason*. The mission-frame absorbs grief, frustration, and pain into productive output. This is the same engine that fuels CPTSD-coded over-functioning, but as a resilience factor it is unmatched: a man with reasons does not break the way men without reasons break.

**2. Internal locus of control — calibrated.** Unusually accurate self-attribution. He neither over-claims agency (the narcissistic failure) nor under-claims it (the depressive failure). He knows what he caused, what he failed to prevent, and what was outside his hands, and he sorts each correctly. This calibration is the single most important psychological hygiene factor in the file.

**3. Reparative parenting as self-repair.** The Hope period did something the years of analysis-equivalent (Askani teaching, mentorship of X-Force) could not: it metabolized the original abandonment by inverting it. He cannot give himself the parent he didn't have, but he could *be* one, and the act partially closed the wound. Post-Hope, the observed depressive substrate is lighter than pre-Hope.

**4. Moral non-negotiables.** A short list of fixed ethical commitments (children are never expendable; lethal force is permissible but never preferential; one does not become Apocalypse to defeat Apocalypse). These do not bend under stress. They function as a keel: he can take heavy weather without capsizing because the bottom of him is weighted.

**5. Humor as pressure valve.** Dry, sparse, self-aware. Easily missed. It is real and it is functional. A man who can be funny about his own circumstances is a man whose circumstances have not entirely consumed him.

**6. Capacity for solitude without decompensation.** He is comfortable alone for extended periods. This is partly defensive (avoidance), but as a resilience trait it means he does not require external regulation to remain stable — a critical asset in a profession that periodically isolates him.

**7. Acceptance of mortality.** Not death-seeking (see Section 4) but death-accepting. He has made his peace with the body's terms. This removes the single largest source of operational paralysis in long-running combatants: fear of one's own ending. He fights cleanly because he is not bargaining.

**8. Updatable identity.** He has, across the record, allowed himself to be *wrong* — about Stryfe, about X-Force methods, about his own messianic role, about his father — and revised. A man who can be wrong and continue is a man whose ego is not the load-bearing structure.

**9. Resurrection redundancy (Krakoan era).** Tactical-grade resilience: death is no longer terminal. He has not been observed to exploit this recklessly — the moral non-negotiables hold — but it removes the worst-case from the operational risk calculus.

**10. The mirror that did not break him.** Stryfe exists. The shadow-self, the not-taken path, the same genome optimized for harm. Cable lives knowing this version of himself is real and external, and he has not collapsed into it, fused with it, or been destroyed by it. The fact of having *held the line against his own worst case* for a lifetime is itself a resilience credential of the rarest kind.

---

## 6.8 What Makes the Asset Stack Durable

Three observations on the *durability* of the above — not just whether he has these strengths but whether they will keep working.

**First: redundancy.** Almost every capability has backup. Lose the techno-organic arm: he has psionics. Lose the psionics: he has tradecraft. Lose the tradecraft: he has the network. Lose the network: he has the timeline. Lose the timeline: he has the moral keel. The stack collapses gracefully rather than catastrophically.

**Second: anti-fragility through prior catastrophe.** He has already lost almost everything that can be lost — parents, body, identity, nation, child, life itself — and reconstituted function from each loss. The base rate of recovery from extreme adverse events, in this subject, is essentially 1.0. Future losses will hurt; they will not end him.

**Third: the asset he most distrusts is himself, which is why he is reliable.** The single best predictor of long-run ethical performance under power is whether the operator considers his own judgment provisional. Cable does. He audits his own decisions, often punitively. This means his assets remain pointed in the direction he claims they're pointed — which, in a subject capable of this much harm, is the only durability that ultimately matters.

---

*End Section 6. Continue to Section 7: Vulnerabilities, Liabilities & Risk Vectors.*


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION

## Subject: Nathan Christopher Charles Summers

---

## 0. Framing: What "Breaking" Means For This Subject

Most operators of comparable history break loudly — substance use, rage spirals, suicidal gesture, dissociative episode, public collapse. The subject does none of these. His failure modes are quiet, structural, and, in the early stages, indistinguishable from competence intensifying. The dossier-relevant insight is that **his decompensation looks, from the outside, like he is getting better at his job.** This is the diagnostic trap. Allies have repeatedly missed his crises because the surface behavior — more planning, more isolation, more personal exposure to risk — reads as professional escalation. It is in fact pathology in late phase.

A second framing point: he has two failure architectures running in parallel. A **somatic** one (the techno-organic virus, which has its own escalation curve independent of his psychology) and a **psychological** one (the CPTSD/dysthymia substrate). They interact. Viral flare-ups consume the telekinetic bandwidth he uses for affect regulation; psychological collapse loosens his cellular control of the virus. Each accelerates the other. There is no clean teasing apart.

---

## 1. The Baseline Steady-State (Stage Zero)

Before describing escalation, the floor: the subject's normal operating condition is already what would constitute, for an ordinary nervous system, a crisis. Sleep two to four hours nightly, often segmented. Resting heart rate elevated for body mass. Continuous low-grade pain. Persistent background telepathic noise filtered by effort. A 24-hour autoimmune campaign run consciously. He is, at any given moment, expending more regulatory energy than most subjects expend in a day.

This means he has **no reserve.** A nervous system already operating at red-line cannot absorb additional load through the usual compensatory routes (extra sleep, withdrawal to recover, comfort behaviors). Every additional stressor is paid for by stealing from another budget — usually the virus-containment budget, occasionally the affect-regulation budget, very rarely the strategic-cognition budget (which he protects above all others, including survival).

The practical surveillance implication: **his early warning signs are subtractive, not additive.** Look for what stops, not what starts.

---

## 2. The Escalation Path

### Phase 1 — Tightening (Days to Weeks)

Onset: typically begins within hours of a triggering event (see Section 5). Outwardly:

- Verbal output drops by an estimated 30–50%. Sentences shorten. Conjunctions disappear. He moves from declaratives to imperatives.
- Humor — the dry, self-deprecating register that is his social lubricant — vanishes first and entirely. This is the most reliable single indicator. When the subject stops making the small, flat jokes at his own expense, the clock has started.
- Posture stiffens; the slight habitual favoring of the right side (compensating for the T-O left) becomes pronounced. He stands more often than he sits.
- Eating becomes purely functional: protein, calories, fast. Coffee intake rises sharply (he is one of the few subjects on whom caffeine still produces detectable acute effect despite chronic use; the body is so suppressed elsewhere that stimulants land hard).
- Sleep contracts further. Below two hours, telepathic bleed-through begins — he picks up ambient thought he would normally filter, which he experiences as a worsening of mood without identifying the cause.
- Tactical planning expands to absorb the slack. He maps contingencies he does not need. He runs drills. He repositions caches. He re-reads files he has memorized.

This phase is *protective in intent* — he is consolidating control to absorb the threat — and *corrosive in effect.* It eats the slack reserves needed for actual recovery and locks him into a stance he cannot release without external intervention.

### Phase 2 — Compartmentalization and Cut-Outs (Weeks to Months)

If the stressor does not resolve, he begins to seal off relationships. Specifically:

- He stops returning communications from anyone he categorizes as "not currently mission-relevant." This includes Scott, the wider X-population, and old allies. He will tell himself he is protecting them; he is in fact narrowing his social surface so that none of it can be leveraged against him or witness his state.
- He begins lying — by omission, never directly — to the inner circle. Domino is the canonical example: he will tell her he is "managing" rather than that he is bleeding capacity to the virus. This is the moment she usually catches it, because she has learned that *managing* is his crisis-vocabulary euphemism.
- Plans become unilateral. He stops running decisions past the team. He frames this internally as efficiency; it is in fact preparation for an action he does not want to be talked out of.
- He begins arranging his affairs: caches inventoried, contingencies left where the right people will find them, a written or recorded message somewhere accessible. Not a suicide note — an after-action package. He has been writing variations of this letter since his twenties.

### Phase 3 — Martyrdom Protocols Engage (Days)

The signature failure mode. Once he has computed that the cost of the problem exceeds what he can ask others to bear, he reaches for the solution structure in which **he is the one paying.** This is not impulsive. It is the cold output of an optimization in which his own continued existence carries a coefficient near zero.

Behavioral markers in this phase:

- He becomes calm. Not flat — *calm.* The tightness releases. Allies who know him register this as the most alarming possible signal: when the subject seems at peace, he has decided to die.
- He becomes generous in small ways uncharacteristic of him. He will sit longer with people. He will say a thing he has not said. He will give away an object. He will use someone's first name.
- He stops protecting the virus boundary. He spends bandwidth he cannot afford on the immediate operation, because there is no longer a future to budget for.
- He maneuvers his allies into positions where they *cannot* intervene at the critical moment — geographic separation, tactical compartmentalization, hard timelines. The most consistent feature of his suicide-equivalent actions is that they are structured to be uninterruptible.

The Hope delivery is the cleanest example: roughly sixteen subjective years of preparation, ending in a final stand that consumed him entirely. But the pattern recurs at smaller scales throughout the record — Providence's surrender, multiple X-Force terminal-stand operations, the Avengers/X-Sanction sequence. The architecture is identical: identify the load only he can bear, arrange to bear it alone, pay it.

### Phase 4 — Post-Survival Collapse (Months to Years)

If he survives a Phase 3 event — which happens, because the body has refused to stay dead and because allies do occasionally breach his cut-outs in time — the subject enters a *delayed* collapse rather than a contemporaneous one. The Soldier X period is the textbook case.

Markers:

- Withdrawal from the field, often geographically extreme (Eastern European wanderings, post-Soviet rural zones, places without comms infrastructure).
- Ascetic rather than indulgent decompensation: he eats little, sleeps rough, owns less, talks to fewer people. There is no hedonic phase.
- Cessation of long-game thinking. He stops planning beyond the day. For him this is equivalent to a normal subject becoming nonverbal — the cognitive function that defines him goes offline.
- Acts of small-scale, anonymous goodness directed at strangers. Read this as a depressed person's attempt to verify, without witnesses, that the mission orientation still holds when stripped of mission. He is checking whether he is still the thing he thought he was.
- Refusal of help when offered. He will not return to allies; allies must come find him, and even then he will frame the reunion as their need, not his.

This is the closest the subject comes to a depressive episode legible to standard psychiatry. It can last months to years. He does not emerge from it through internal recovery; he emerges when a new mission presents itself and he can re-organize around it. The depression does not lift — it gets a job.

---

## 3. Decompensation Signatures by Domain

**Linguistic.** Sentence length collapses. Code-switching from contemporary English to Askani'son cadences (more archaic syntax, more imperative mood) when stress is high — a regression to the language environment of formative trauma. Use of the second-person impersonal ("you do what's needed") replaces first-person under load.

**Motor.** The slight left-side favoring becomes a pronounced guard. He stops gesturing with the T-O hand. He sits with the left side toward walls when possible. Micro-tremor in the right hand under sustained stress (clean hand carries the load the augmented one used to). Increased reliance on the cybernetic eye for tactical scanning even in non-tactical environments — he is checking corners in living rooms.

**Telepathic/Telekinetic.** Sub-threshold ambient bleed: lights flicker near him under acute stress; small ungrasped objects shift millimeters. He does not notice. Allies sometimes do. When the bleed becomes visible, the virus containment is borrowing from the wrong account and he has perhaps 72 hours before somatic crisis.

**Somatic.** Visible T-O progression in observable zones (the eye socket, the jawline, the dorsal hand) is the lagging indicator. When new circuitry-bloom is visible to the naked eye, the psychological crisis is at least two weeks old. The body publishes the news last.

**Relational.** Reduction in mentorship behaviors. He stops correcting younger operatives, stops offering the small tactical asides that constitute his primary expression of care. When the teaching stops, the patient is critical.

---

## 4. Failure Modes by Type

### 4a. The Mission-Substituted Suicide
Described above (Phase 3). Most common terminal failure. He does not call it suicide and would reject the framing; the operational structure is nonetheless self-terminating. Probability of recurrence: high, and structurally so — every time he is given sole-bearer responsibility for a stake he categorizes as transcendent, the protocol engages. The only known interruption is the presence of a *successor* he trusts to carry the load. Hope is the unique case study: once she existed, the protocol shifted from "die delivering" to "die delivering *her*," which is the same protocol with a different payload.

### 4b. The Ascetic Withdrawal
Phase 4 above. Survivable, recoverable, but with permanent erosion each cycle. Each Soldier X-equivalent period leaves him slightly more depressive at baseline and slightly less able to access the warmth he was already rationing.

### 4c. The Stryfe Intrusion
The subject's most specifically intrapsychic failure. Under acute identity stress — typically clone-related, time-travel-related, or origin-related events — the externalized bad-self that is Stryfe re-emerges as intrusive cognition, possibly true psionic contamination, possibly indistinguishable from PTSD-flashback proper. The subject's defense is to treat all such intrusion as enemy action requiring tactical response, which is sometimes correct and sometimes a categorization error costing him weeks of misdirected effort. He has never, on record, accepted the framing that Stryfe is *also* a part of him to be integrated rather than defeated. This refusal is itself a failure mode and the most likely long-term vulnerability.

### 4d. The Reproduction-of-Apocalypse Vertigo
When confronted credibly — usually by an ally, occasionally by his own observation — with the fact that his methods (child soldiers, preemptive lethality, secrecy from the protected) reproduce the methods of the system that made him, the subject does not deflect, rationalize, or rage. He absorbs. He goes quiet for hours to days. Then he resumes the methods. The collapse here is not behavioral but moral: he has accepted the indictment and chosen to continue, which is a more corrosive position than either denial or reform. Each cycle of this deepens the depressive substrate. It is the single greatest contributor to the "used instrument" self-concept.

### 4e. The Handled-By-Allies Trust Fracture
When he detects that an ally has been managing him — withholding information for his own good, coordinating behind his back, treating him as fragile — the response is immediate and disproportionate. He cuts the ally out cleanly, with no scene. Repair takes months and sometimes does not happen. This is not pride; it is the original wound. Being decided-for is the structure of every primary betrayal in his life (the surrender to Askani, the extraction of Slym and Redd, the Apocalypse selection, the Stryfe substitution). His system reads "we made a call for you" as the signal of imminent abandonment and pre-empts.

### 4f. The Caretaking Refusal
Offers of rest, sanctuary, retirement, or recuperative attention produce a stereotyped withdrawal. He will leave the room, the building, the country. He cannot metabolize being taken care of. The internal experience, derived from behavioral pattern, is something like: *if I accept this, I become the kind of thing that can be taken care of, and the kind of thing that can be taken care of is the kind of thing that gets given away.* The defense is to remain perpetually the caretaker. Failure mode: he becomes unreachable precisely when the people around him have correctly identified that he needs reaching.

---

## 5. The Triggering Conditions

In rough order of reliability:

1. **A child placed in his protection.** Universally activates the full pattern. The Hope sequence is the diagnostic exemplar; smaller analogues recur with younger X-Force members, with versions of his younger self, with refugees in the Providence period. The protective response is unconditional and the cost is always paid out of his own reserve.
2. **Direct contact with Apocalypse, Stryfe, or clone/time-doppelgänger material.** Triggers identity-vertigo and the Stryfe-intrusion failure mode. He cannot encounter his mirror without paying for it psychologically for weeks.
3. **Being lied to or managed by an ally he trusted.** Trust fracture, near-instant.
4. **A credible argument that his methods are Apocalyptic.** Moral collapse without behavioral change.
5. **Loss of the virus-containment margin.** Either because the virus surges or because he has had to spend bandwidth elsewhere. This collapses everything else because the virus is the floor everything sits on.
6. **Offers of rest from people he loves.** The caretaking refusal. The cruel irony: the more sincerely it is offered, the more violently he must refuse.
7. **Forced peer position.** Being placed in a relationship structure where he cannot be the senior partner — teacher, commander, father, protector. Marriage-equivalent intimacy, in particular, he cannot sustain. The relationships that have lasted have all had role-asymmetry built in.
8. **Prolonged peace.** Underrated. Mission-absence does not relax him; it removes the structure that organizes the depression. Sustained periods without a war produce drift, then withdrawal, then a sought-out mission, then relief.

---

## 6. What Recovery Looks Like (and Why It Is Partial)

Full remission has never been observed in the record and is unlikely to be possible given the somatic substrate. What does occur:

- **Mission-organized functionality.** When properly oriented toward a stake he believes only he can carry, he is one of the highest-functioning operators on record. The depression is present but harnessed.
- **Reparative parenting episodes.** The Hope period demonstrated that giving him a long-duration protective role for a single child, in conditions resembling his own origin, allows him to do live in-vivo trauma work without the framing of therapy. He emerged from those sixteen years more integrated than he entered them — though he then spent the integration to deliver her.
- **Domino-mediated stabilization.** The one peer-adjacent relationship that has consistently de-escalated him. She does not try to make him rest; she stays present while he doesn't. This is the only model of care he can tolerate.
- **Mentorship of younger versions of himself.** Late-period appearances with adolescent counterparts (Kid Cable arc and aftermath) show the subject attempting to extend to his earlier self the protection he could not extend to himself contemporaneously. Whether this is recovery or another iteration of the asymmetric-care defense is unclear; both readings are defensible.

What does *not* work: rest, sanctuary, therapy in any formal sense, peer marriage-equivalent intimacy, retirement, removal from threat environments. Each of these accelerates rather than reverses decompensation, because each removes the mission scaffolding that holds the structure up.

---

## 7. The Terminal Prediction

Absent successful integration of the Stryfe-self (which he has historically refused) and absent a permanent successor (Hope discharged that function once but is now an adult peer), the subject's terminal failure mode is functionally locked in: a Phase 3 martyrdom event, executed cleanly, in service of a stake he has decided only he can carry, with allies geographically and tactically excluded from intervention. He has rehearsed this end across a forty-year publication record. He has performed it in full at least once. He has been resurrected, in various forms, several times. The recurrence is not coincidence; the system that produces him keeps generating the conditions, and his nervous system keeps generating the response.

The honest dossier conclusion: he is not a subject one *fixes.* He is a subject one *witnesses,* with the understanding that the witnessing is itself a form of care he can occasionally tolerate, and that the most respectful intervention available is to ensure that when he next pays the price he has been preparing to pay since infancy, someone present knows what was paid, and for whom, and why.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 11

## TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT

*Subject: Nathan Christopher Charles Summers*
*Horizon: 12 months tactical / 5 years strategic / lifetime arc*
*Confidence: Moderate-to-high on near-term behavioral prediction; lower on geopolitical and somatic variables, which are coupled and volatile.*

---

### 11.1 The Shape of the Curve

Forecasting this subject is unusual in that he himself forecasts professionally, has lived in multiple futures, and structures his present around averting specific ones. He is therefore a *reflexive* prediction problem: any reading we offer he has likely already considered, weighted, and either accepted or routed around. The analytical task is not to outguess him — that game is unwinnable — but to map the structural constraints he cannot strategize his way out of, and to identify the fork points at which the unconscious material will overrun the strategic apparatus.

The headline finding: **Cable's trajectory is converging, not diverging.** After three decades of widening ambition (squad → army → floating nation → savior-of-the-mutant-line), the arc has begun to spiral inward. Each successive mission is more personal, more parental, more concerned with a single life rather than a population. This is not retreat. It is the late-career narrowing of a man who has concluded that the only victories he trusts are the ones he can hold in his arms. Expect this to continue.

---

### 11.2 The Somatic Clock

Every other trajectory question is dominated by one variable: **the techno-organic viral load and his remaining telekinetic margin to suppress it.**

- **Baseline trajectory:** The virus is progressive; suppression cost rises monotonically with age, stress, and physical injury. He is, in effect, on a balance sheet where the liability column compounds and the asset column (psionic capacity, neural plasticity, cellular reserve) erodes.
- **Inflection signals to monitor:** spread visible past the left clavicle to the sternum; involvement of the right hand or jaw; any episode of involuntary T-O extrusion under stress (a phenomenon previously associated with terminal phase); reduction in fine telekinetic work (the diagnostic test is whether he can still field-strip a sidearm telekinetically — when that drops, the margin is gone).
- **The Hope-equivalent collapse:** during the sixteen-year flight with the infant, his body was visibly losing the war by the end. He should be presumed to have a hard ceiling — perhaps a decade, perhaps less — before he will again face a choice between mission-burn and slow conversion.
- **Behavioral consequence:** A man with a body-clock organizes his life around legacy. Expect accelerated mentorship behavior, accelerated reconciliation gestures (particularly toward Scott), and an increased willingness to take terminal-risk missions on the implicit logic that the alternative is dying slower in a chair.

The somatic clock is also the leash on his strategic horizon. He plans in decades but lives in months. This tension — long-game cognition in a short-runway body — is the engine of every escalation we will see from him.

---

### 11.3 Likely Developments — 12-Month Horizon

**High probability (>70%):**

- **Continued mentor-pattern recruitment.** He will identify, observe, and tactically adopt one or two younger combatants — quietly, without ceremony, often without their immediate knowledge that they have been folded into his long-term planning. The pattern is consistent across X-Force, the Six Pack reformations, the New Mutants leadership, and the Hope years.
- **At least one unsanctioned solo operation.** He runs a parallel mission queue outside any institutional sanction. The trigger is invariably intelligence — usually time-displaced — that he cannot or will not share with allies because sharing would require explaining the source.
- **A confrontation with the younger version of himself (Kid Cable / temporal counterpart).** The intrapsychic content here is not optional; it will surface. Whether it resolves through dialogue, combat, or merger depends on which of them is more willing to abandon the script.
- **One quiet medical crisis, concealed.** He will lose suppression margin acutely — probably under combat load or psionic strain — and will not disclose it to Domino, to Scott, or to medical. The concealment is reflexive; he experiences disclosure as the prelude to being managed.

**Moderate probability (40–70%):**

- A return engagement with the Stryfe-vector — either the original consciousness re-emerging, a Stryfe-coded antagonist, or an Apocalypse-lineage actor who triggers the same intrapsychic architecture. The probability is not low because the structure demands the mirror; narrative gravity is in this case a real intelligence signal about the subject's own pattern-seeking.
- A short, deliberate retreat — a week, a month — to a location with no comms (historical preference: high-altitude rural, sparse human density, manual labor available). Read as decompression, not depression; distinguish from a Soldier-X-pattern wandering, which is longer, less purposeful, and signals a deeper collapse.
- An attempt at a structured conversation with Scott Summers in which both men try, and partly fail, to occupy the correct generational roles. Outcome will be ambiguous; the affective residue will be productive.

**Lower probability but high-impact (15–40%):**

- A founding act — a school, a clinic, a small sovereign project — that is functionally Providence-in-miniature. Smaller scale than the original, because he has learned. Still doomed in the medium term, because he has not learned *enough*.
- Public disclosure, partial, of the prophetic / Askani frame to a peer he trusts. This would be a significant shift. The candidate is Domino; the second candidate is Hope.

---

### 11.4 The Five-Year Strategic Outlook

Over a five-year window, three structural pressures will compound:

**(a) The reparative-parenting cycle is incomplete.** Hope was the breakthrough — the first relationship in which he gave without dominance because the asymmetry was developmentally appropriate. But Hope is now an adult, and the asymmetry has dissolved, which means the relationship has moved into territory he has never successfully held: *equal-peer* with someone he loves. Watch for awkwardness, over-instruction, withdrawal, and eventually — if he does the work — a slow conversion to adult friendship. If he does not do the work, he will recruit a new child to re-stage the dynamic. Predict the latter unless actively interrupted.

**(b) The Scott-Summers reconciliation window is closing.** Father and son have circled each other for decades without ever stabilizing the role assignment. Both are operationally similar (strategic, sacrificial, mission-coded), which is why they cannot rest together — each reads the other's tactics as a critique. The five-year window will produce either a hard rapprochement (probable trigger: a crisis in which one saves the other at cost) or a permanent armistice in which they cooperate well and never speak of anything personal. The latter is the more likely outcome and is, by his standards, an acceptable one.

**(c) The Apocalypse-shadow problem will not stay buried.** As long as the principle of *designing children as weapons* exists in the world — and post-Krakoan biotech, resurrection protocols, and ongoing genetic engineering ensure that it does — Cable's central enemy is structural, not personal. He will at some point realize, if he has not already fully metabolized it, that there is no individual he can kill to end this. The realization will produce either his most generative phase (systemic reform work; advocacy; legal/political engagement, which would be entirely out of pattern but not impossible) or his most depressive (the Soldier-X attractor, deepened by age).

---

### 11.5 The Lifetime Arc

He is in late career. The arc that remains is not about acquisition — of skills, missions, allies, territory — but about disposition: what he sets down, what he hands off, and what he writes into other people before the suppression margin closes.

The lifetime question, stripped to one sentence: **Can he accept being cared for before he dies?**

Every other developmental task is downstream of this. The capacity to be cared for is the capacity to receive without converting the gift into a debt to be repaid by service. It is the one psychological move he has never made. Hope can give it to him. Domino has tried. Scott has tried, badly. If he can take it from any of them — even once, even briefly — the rest of the work becomes available: real grief, real rest, the metabolization of the rage he has never processed, the relinquishment of the prophetic frame as *his* burden rather than as a role he carries on behalf of a future he no longer believes is fixed.

If he cannot, the arc ends as the early ones did: in a sacrificial act, well-executed, calibrated to maximize the survival of the people behind him, with the suppression margin spent in one final operational push. It would not be a tragedy by his own metric — by his metric it would be a successful conclusion — and that is precisely the problem the assessment must flag.

---

### 11.6 The Open Questions

These are the items the file cannot resolve and which any future custodian of this dossier should treat as live:

1. **Has the prophetic identification been retired, suppressed, or merely re-framed?** He no longer speaks the messianic vocabulary, but the behavior — building, saving, dying for — is unchanged. We cannot tell from outside whether he has actually grown past the role or only updated the rhetoric. The test: confront him with a situation in which the *correct* prophetic move would be inaction. Observe.

2. **What is the actual telepathic ceiling if the virus is removed?** Every estimate is theoretical. There is a non-trivial possibility that decades of cellular-level suppression work have re-shaped his psionic architecture in ways that would not simply rebound to baseline if the disease were cured. He may be, structurally, a being whose powers exist only in the negative — defined by what they hold back. A cure could produce capacity he cannot govern. He has likely modeled this and decided he prefers the disease.

3. **Is the Stryfe-content fully externalized, or is there integration work pending?** The clinical literature on splitting suggests the externalized bad-object tends to return if the host self is not consolidated. Stryfe-as-person is intermittently active; Stryfe-as-internal-figure has never been worked through. The integration, if it occurs, will not look like victory. It will look like the subject being able to say *what he and Stryfe shared* without flinching.

4. **What happens to him when the wars end?** The Krakoan settlement, the various armistices, the periodic mutant-political stabilizations all raise the question. He has no peacetime identity. We have no data on him at rest because he has never been at rest. The prediction is that he would deteriorate within months — not from boredom but from the absence of a frame that justifies the suppression cost. He needs an enemy to keep his body running.

5. **Will he ever let the temporal counterpart live as a separate person?** The presence of a younger version of himself in the same continuity is psychologically intolerable on its current terms — each is the other's reproach. Either they merge, one supplants the other, or they negotiate a separation that is genuinely two lives. The third outcome is the healthiest and the least likely.

---

### 11.7 The Fork Points

Specific, identifiable inflection events at which the trajectory could be redirected. Each is given with the *push toward growth* condition and the *push toward catastrophe* condition.

**Fork 1: The next somatic crisis.**
- *Growth:* He discloses it, accepts intervention, allows a peer to share the suppression load (if such a thing is even possible — Hope's potential is the wildcard here). Establishes a precedent for being helped.
- *Catastrophe:* He conceals it, compensates, and treats the incident as evidence that his timeline is shorter than projected, which accelerates every other martyrdom protocol.

**Fork 2: The next child-in-danger scenario.**
- *Growth:* He coordinates, delegates, supports the operation without occupying the lead role. Demonstrates that the pattern can be acted on without him being the one to absorb the cost.
- *Catastrophe:* He repeats the Hope protocol — extracts the child, isolates with the child, reproduces his own childhood inverted. The mission succeeds; the subject loses another five years of suppression margin and another developmental window.

**Fork 3: The Scott-Summers crisis event.**
- *Growth:* Whichever one of them is saved by the other accepts the salvation without converting it into a strategic debt. The role of "son" or "father" is occupied honestly, however briefly. The reconciliation does not require words.
- *Catastrophe:* One dies for the other under conditions that prevent the survivor from completing the relationship. Probability non-trivial; both men volunteer for terminal risk as a matter of operational default.

**Fork 4: The peace.**
- *Growth:* He builds a non-combat role — teaching, writing the war down, formal mentorship in a settled institution — that gives the suppression machinery a non-military justification. This would be unprecedented and would constitute the deepest structural change available to him.
- *Catastrophe:* He invents a war. Identifies a threat, real or constructed-from-fragments, that justifies the resumption of operations. This is the Providence pattern at a smaller scale.

**Fork 5: The Stryfe-return.**
- *Growth:* He engages the encounter with curiosity about what they share rather than only what divides them. Does not kill the mirror; does not need to.
- *Catastrophe:* The encounter triggers the splitting defense at full strength. He becomes briefly more lethal, more isolated, and less reachable than at any point since the Soldier-X period. Collateral damage to allies is the risk.

**Fork 6: Domino's exit, by any cause.**
- *Growth:* He grieves openly to one other person. Any one. The historical record suggests he has never done this and the inhibition is the load-bearing wall of the entire defensive structure. A single instance would change the building.
- *Catastrophe:* He metabolizes the loss the way he has metabolized every prior loss — by absorbing it into mission. The cost is invisible to outside observers and will surface, if at all, as a sudden downward step in functional baseline six to eighteen months later.

---

### 11.8 What Would Move Him

For any future actor — ally, clinician, family member, institutional custodian — attempting to support this subject's growth rather than merely his operational continuity, the following are the leverage points, ranked by realistic accessibility:

1. **Hope Summers, as adult peer.** She is the only person whose authority over his emotional life is non-negotiable, because the love is non-negotiable and she knows it. She is also the only person who has seen him *parent* and can therefore call him to the standard he set for himself. If anyone gets him to rest, it will be her, and the mechanism will be her refusing to accept his death as a gift.
2. **A medical intervention he did not author.** The pattern of refusing care is broken only by being given care he could not refuse — i.e., delivered while unconscious by someone he trusts not to compromise his autonomy in any other way. The precedent, once set, cracks the counter-dependence.
3. **A confrontation, by someone he respects, with the X-Force critique.** He has internalized it but never had to answer for it out loud to a peer who would not let him deflect. The conversation would be the hardest thing he has ever sat through. It would also be the most productive.
4. **A non-instrumental relationship.** Any sustained connection with a person who has *no mission use* and no need of his protection. He has not had one in his adult life. The prediction is that he would experience it initially as suspicious, then as boring, then as a place he keeps returning to without knowing why.
5. **Writing.** A long-shot recommendation. He has the cognitive bandwidth, the historical perspective, and the unprocessed material. A private record — not for publication, not for tactical use, simply for the act — would do work that no conversation has yet done. There is no evidence he has ever considered it. There is also no evidence he would refuse.

---

### 11.9 What Would Break Him

For completeness, and because the file must include the failure modes:

- **The death of Hope** under conditions in which he could plausibly have prevented it. Predicted outcome: a Soldier-X period of unprecedented length and depth, terminating in either ascetic disappearance or a single terminal mission.
- **A successful Apocalypse-lineage actor producing another designed child.** Re-triggers every formative wound at once. Predicted response: monomaniacal pursuit, methods escalation, alienation of allies.
- **Sustained, unwanted protection by allies who think they know better.** Specifically: a Krakoan-style or institutional decision to medically intervene, retire him from operations, or override his strategic judgment in his interest. Predicted response: exit. He will leave whatever institution does this, regardless of what he loses by leaving.
- **The discovery that one of his long-game timeline interventions caused, rather than prevented, a catastrophe.** This is the existential risk to his entire operating identity. He has structured his life around the premise that intervention is justified by averted harm. A confirmed reversal would destabilize the foundation. Predicted response, depending on severity: deep depressive episode, withdrawal from time-travel methods, or — at the worst — an attempt to undo the intervention that produced a still-worse outcome (the recursive failure mode).

---

### 11.10 Bottom Line for the File

He will not retire. He will not be cured. He will not, on his own initiative, ask for help. He will continue to do the work — competently, ethically, at increasing personal cost — until either the suppression margin closes or someone he loves refuses to let him spend it. The probability that someone refuses is non-zero and is, in our assessment, the single variable on which the late arc turns.

If he is given one more decade in which to do the integration work — and if Hope, Domino, or Scott can break through on even one of the load-bearing defenses — he ends as a teacher, a grandfather-figure to the next mutant generation, and a man who has finally taken his own measure without flinching. The historical comparison is to elder statesmen of liberation movements who outlived the war and learned, late, how to live in the peace they made.

If he is not, he ends as he has ended before, and the only question will be which child he was carrying when he stopped.

— END SECTION 11 —
